## LLM适合量子软件、架构和系统设计吗？

**Original Title:** Are LLMs Good For Quantum Software, Architecture, and System Design?

**Authors:** Sourish Wawdhane, Poulami Das

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.26904v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.26904v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-27


### 摘要

量子计算机有望为物理、化学、密码分析、医疗保健等许多关键领域的问题带来巨大的计算加速。然而，尽管经过了数十年的研究，它们仍然远未进入实用时代。缺乏能够将算法的量子力学特性转化为量子位设备上的物理状态转换的成熟软件、架构和系统解决方案仍然是技术进步缓慢的关键因素。由于严重依赖特定领域的专业知识，特别是对于软件开发人员、计算机架构师和系统工程师来说，问题变得更加严重。为了解决这些限制并加速大规模高性能量子系统设计，我们提出以下问题：   大型语言模型（LLM）能否帮助解决量子软件、架构和系统问题？   在这项工作中，我们提出了一个案例研究，评估LLM在量子系统推理任务上的性能。我们评估了九个前沿法学硕士，并将它们与德州大学奥斯汀分校的毕业生在一系列量子计算问题上的表现进行了比较。最后，我们推荐了研究和工程开发工作必须遵循的几个方向。


### Abstract

Quantum computers promise massive computational speedup for problems in many critical domains, such as physics, chemistry, cryptanalysis, healthcare, etc. However, despite decades of research, they remain far from entering an era of utility. The lack of mature software, architecture, and systems solutions capable of translating quantum-mechanical properties of algorithms into physical state transformations on qubit devices remains a key factor underlying the slow pace of technological progress. The problem worsens due to significant reliance on domain-specific expertise, especially for software developers, computer architects, and systems engineers. To address these limitations and accelerate large-scale high-performance quantum system design, we ask:
  Can large language models (LLMs) help with solving quantum software, architecture, and systems problems?
  In this work, we present a case study assessing the performance of LLMs on quantum system reasoning tasks. We evaluate nine frontier LLMs and compare their performance to graduate UT Austin students on a set of quantum computing problems. Finally, we recommend several directions along which research and engineering development efforts must be pursued.


---


## 无籽QRNG引导和混合PQC-QKD密钥组合的信息论解决方案

**Original Title:** Information-Theoretic Solutions for Seedless QRNG Bootstrapping and Hybrid PQC-QKD Key Combination

**Authors:** Juan Antonio Vieira Giestinhas, Timothy Spiller

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.26907v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.26907v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-27


### 摘要

本文考虑了实际量子网络面临的两个挑战：无籽量子随机数发生器（QRNG）的自举和后量子密码学（PQC）和量子密钥分发（QKD）密钥的弹性组合。这些问题是使用通用哈希函数作为强种子提取器来解决的，其安全基础由量子剩余哈希引理（QLHL）提供。首先，在QRNG中的“随机性循环”-初始随机种子产生进一步的随机性的要求-通过提出一种使用来自两个独立的熵源的原始数据的自举方法来解决，所述熵源由无籽QRNG源给出。其次，有人认为，强种子提取器是一种替代XOR为基础的关键组合，呈现出不同的特点。与异或不同，我们的方法确保如果组合输出和一个初始密钥受到损害，剩余的密钥材料保留可量化的最小熵，并且在交换更长的密钥时保持安全。此外，所提出的方法允许以自然的方式将笔录信息与关键材料绑定，提供了一种工具来取代基于计算的组合器，以将初始关键材料的ITS安全性扩展到最终组合输出。通过将PQC密钥建模为具有HILL（Hastad、Impagliazzo、Levin和Luby）熵，该框架被扩展到混合PQC-QKD系统。这种统一的方法提供了数学上严格且面向未来的机制，用于随机性生成和针对量子对手的安全密钥管理。


### Abstract

This paper considers two challenges faced by practical quantum networks: the bootstrapping of seedless Quantum Random Number Generators (QRNGs) and the resilient combination of Post-Quantum Cryptography (PQC) and Quantum Key Distribution (QKD) keys. These issues are addressed using universal hash functions as strong seeded extractors, with security foundations provided by the Quantum Leftover Hash Lemma (QLHL). First, the 'randomness loop' in QRNGs -- the requirement of an initial random seed to generate further randomness -- is resolved by proposing a bootstrapping method using raw data from two independent sources of entropy, given by seedless QRNG sources. Second, it is argued that strong seeded extractors are an alternative to XOR-based key combining that presents different characteristics. Unlike XORing, our method ensures that if the combined output and one initial key are compromised, the remaining key material retains quantifiable min-entropy and remains secure in exchange of longer keys. Furthermore, the proposed method allows to bind transcript information with key material in a natural way, providing a tool to replace computationally based combiners to extend ITS security of the initial key material to the final combined output. By modeling PQC keys as having HILL (Hastad, Impagliazzo, Levin and Luby) entropy, the framework is extended to hybrid PQC-QKD systems. This unified approach provides a mathematically rigorous and future-proof mechanism for both randomness generation and secure key management against quantum adversaries.


---


## 极化场项在腔量子材料模型中的作用

**Original Title:** The role of polarization field terms in a model for a cavity quantum material

**Authors:** Arwen Lloyd, Adam Stokes, Alessandro Principi, Ahsan Nazir

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.26917v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.26917v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-27


### 摘要

构建腔量子材料模型需要仔细处理光物质耦合。一般来说，必须指定从物质波函数构建的矩阵元素，而物质波函数在紧约束框架中通常是未知的。在低能量理论中可以忽略带内和带间DMZ的贡献的假设下，通常使用Peierls替代来避免在多中心偶极（或Peiels）规范中引入这些额外参数。我们在典型变换的被动观点中提出了皮尔斯规范描述的推导。我们构建了一个玩具模型的多波段系统有两个网站，我们耦合到一个均匀的库仑场，偶极子，和佩尔斯规范。我们发现，Peierls替代可以被证明是一个低能量，有效的单带描述在一维，但它错过了自极化校正和直接耦合需要描述带间跃迁在完整的Peierls规范理论。此外，库仑、偶极子和佩尔斯规范将复合系统划分为光和物质子系统。我们说明了这个子系统的物理观测量和轨道截断在每个规范的性能相对论的影响。


### Abstract

Constructing models for cavity quantum materials requires a careful treatment of the light-matter coupling. In general, one must specify matrix elements constructed from the material wavefunctions, which are often unknown in a tight-binding framework. The Peierls substitution is often used to avoid introducing these additional parameters in the multi-center dipole (or Peiels) gauge, under the assumption that contributions from intraband and interband dipole moments can be neglected in the low-energy theory. We present the derivation of the Peierls gauge description in the passive view of canonical transformations. We construct a toy model for a multi-band system with two sites, which we couple to a uniform field in the Coulomb, dipole, and Peierls gauges. We find that the Peierls substitution can be justified as a low-energy, effectively single-band description in one dimension, but it misses both self-polarization corrections and the direct coupling needed to describe interband transitions in the full Peierls gauge theory. Moreover, the Coulomb, dipole, and Peierls gauges define distinct partitions of the composite system into the light and matter subsystems. We illustrate the implications of this subsystem relativity for physical observables and on the performance of orbital truncations in each gauge.


---


## 用弱测量监测量子行走

**Original Title:** Monitoring of quantum walks with weak measurements

**Authors:** Klaus Ziegler, Tim Heine, Sabine Tornow

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.26933v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.26933v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-27


### 摘要

测量可用于监控量子系统的演变，并可产生量化回报统计。众所周知，平均返回时间是通过被监测量子状态的缠绕数进行量化的，以进行强监测。我们讨论了在通过辅助耦合实现的连贯弱监测下，量子行走的平均返回时间相对于测量强度服从比例关系。之前发现了随机时间监测的模拟比例关系，表明弱监测和随机时间监测具有相似的效果。我们讨论了通过辅助耦合的弱监测如何与单一进化联系起来，以及如何通过收敛微扰理论控制这种联系。


### Abstract

Measurements can be used to monitor the evolution of quantum systems and can give rise to quantized return statistics. It is known that the mean return time is quantized for strong monitoring through the winding number of the monitored quantum state. We discuss that under coherent weak monitoring, implemented via ancilla coupling, the mean return time of a quantum walk obeys a scaling relation with respect to the measurement strength. An analog scaling relation was previously found for random-time monitoring, indicating that weak and random-time monitoring have similar effects. We discuss how weak monitoring via ancilla coupling is linked to the unitary evolution, and how this connection can be controlled by a convergent perturbation theory.


---


## 广义Caldeira-Leggett模型的热脱水

**Original Title:** Thermoforesis from generalized Caldeira-Leggett models

**Authors:** Daniel Valente, Maurício Matos, Thiago Werlang

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.26980v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.26980v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-27


### 摘要

标准的Caldeira-Leggett模型解决了热平衡环境中的布朗运动问题。在这里，我们寻找Caldeira-Leggett模型的推广来解释环境中的热梯度。我们设计了两种类型的模型，并讨论了每种模型的优点和局限性。从这两个模型中，我们发现了热泳的特征，即，由于热梯度导致的粒子传输。原则上，我们的模型可以用于描述量子布朗粒子中的热泳现象，这是迄今为止的一个悬而未决的问题。


### Abstract

The standard Caldeira-Leggett model addresses the problem of Brownian motion in a thermal equilibrium environment. Here, we look for generalizations of the Caldeira-Leggett model to account for thermal gradients in the environment. We devise two types of models, and discuss the advantages and limitations of each one. From both models, we find signatures of thermophoresis, i.e., particle transport due to a thermal gradient. In principle, our models can be employed to describe thermophoresis in quantum Brownian particles, an open problem so far.

## 基于故障测量的量子计算的双曲团态

**Original Title:** Hyperbolic Cluster States for Fault-Tolerant Measurement-Based Quantum Computing

**Authors:** Ahmed Adel Mahmoud, Gabrielle Tournaire, Sven Bachmann, Steven Rayan

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27004v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.27004v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-27


### 摘要

基于故障测量的量子计算（MBQC）为故障量子计算提供了一个令人信服的框架，其中量子信息通过对称为集群状态的三维纠缠资源的单量子位测量来处理。到目前为止，该资源主要是在欧几里得格上研究的，最引人注目的是在Raussendorf-Harrington-Goyal（RHG）构造中，该构造是MBQC中的拓扑故障容忍的基础。在这项工作中，我们引入了双曲团团态，这是三维团团态对负弯曲几何的推广，通过周期性双曲格子的叶理获得。我们提出了双曲团簇状态的显式构造，并在现实的电路级去极化噪音模型下研究了它们的耐故障特性。使用大规模的数值模拟，我们进行内存实验，以表征其逻辑错误率和解码性能。我们的研究结果表明，双曲集群状态表现出容错阈值可比的欧几里得RHG集群状态，同时支持一个恒定的编码率在热力学极限。这表示相对于传统的簇状态构造，量子比特开销有了实质性的改善。这些发现建立双曲几何作为一个强大的和实验相关的资源，可扩展的，容错的MBQC和开放的新途径，利用负曲率的量子信息处理。


### Abstract

Fault-tolerant measurement-based quantum computing (MBQC) provides a compelling framework for fault-tolerant quantum computation, in which quantum information is processed through single-qubit measurements on a three-dimensional entangled resource known as cluster state. To date, this resource has been predominantly studied on Euclidean lattices, most notably in the Raussendorf-Harrington-Goyal (RHG) construction, which underlies topological fault tolerance in MBQC. In this work, we introduce the hyperbolic cluster state, a generalization of the three-dimensional cluster state to negatively curved geometries, obtained via the foliation of periodic hyperbolic lattices. We present an explicit construction of hyperbolic cluster states and investigate their fault-tolerant properties under a realistic circuit-level depolarizing noise model. Using large-scale numerical simulations, we perform memory experiments to characterize their logical error rates and decoding performance. Our results demonstrate that hyperbolic cluster states exhibit a fault-tolerance threshold comparable to that of the Euclidean RHG cluster state, while simultaneously supporting a constant encoding rate in the thermodynamic limit. This represents a substantial improvement in qubit overhead relative to conventional cluster-state constructions. These findings establish hyperbolic geometry as a powerful and experimentally relevant resource for scalable, fault-tolerant MBQC and open new avenues for leveraging negative curvature in quantum information processing.


---


## 二维拓扑绝缘子中琐碎状态的非单位制备非平凡状态

**Original Title:** Nonunitary Preparation of Nontrivial States from Trivial Regimes in Two-Dimensional Topological Insulators

**Authors:** Qin-Qin Wang, Xiao-Ye Xu, Chuan-Feng Li, Guang-Can Guo

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27028v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.27028v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-27


### 摘要

虽然在广泛的物理平台上设计非平凡的汉密尔顿体方面取得了显着的进展，但准备其相应的非平凡的基本状态仍然是一个重大的实验挑战。常用的状态准备策略依赖于隔热协议。然而，当一个平凡的初始状态被整体驱动到非平凡的状态时，动力学必须跨越间隙闭合临界点，使该过程本质上是非隔热的，并且该状态仍然是平凡的。在这里，我们提出了一种在二维拓扑绝缘体中动态制备非平凡状态的非正方法。通过将去相噪音引入缓慢驱动的正进化中，我们证明了所产生的去相状态的拓扑数可以与目标非平凡Hamilton的拓扑数一致。这种近乎隔热的非正状态准备协议为访问拓扑状态的传统隔热方法提供了强大的替代方案。


### Abstract

While remarkable progress has been achieved in engineering nontrivial Hamiltonians across a wide range of physical platforms, preparing their corresponding nontrivial ground states remains a major experimental challenge. The commonly used strategy for state preparation relies on adiabatic protocols. However, when a trivial initial state is unitarily driven toward nontrivial regimes, the dynamics must cross gap-closing critical points, rendering the process intrinsically nonadiabatic, and the state remains topologically trivial. Here, we present a nonunitary method for dynamically preparing nontrivial states in two-dimensional topological insulators. By introducing dephasing noise into a slowly driven unitary evolution, we demonstrate that the topological number of the resulting dephased states can coincide with that of the target nontrivial Hamiltonian. This nearly adiabatic nonunitary state-preparation protocol provides a powerful alternative to conventional adiabatic approaches for accessing topological states.


---


## 超宽带、低损耗波合路器和滤光片：薄膜Niobate锂的新颖设计和实验

**Original Title:** Ultra-broadband, Low-loss Wavelength Combiners and Filters: Novel Designs and Experiments in Thin-film Lithium Niobate

**Authors:** Robert Kwolek, Parash Thapalia, Aditya Tripathi, Pooja Kulkarni, Jaber Balalhabashi, Farzaneh Arab Juneghani, Michael Bullock Oanh Hoang Vo, Sasan Fathpour, Rajveer Nehra

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27034v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.27034v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-27


### 摘要

薄膜锂酸盐（TFLN）已经成为量子和经典应用的大规模可编程光子电路的领先平台。随着电路复杂性的增加，宽带泵浦和信号场的低损耗路由变得至关重要。在这里，我们提出了封闭形式的分析模型和实验证明紧凑，快速准绝热驱动优化波长组合器和滤波器工作在基波（FH，1550 nm）和二次谐波（SH，775 nm）波长。我们的设计在90 nm带宽上实现了低于0.06 dB的超低损耗，同时保持消光比超过25 dB。在SH处，在45纳米带宽内，损耗保持在0.12分贝以下，并且熄灭比大于19分贝。在300纳米TFLN平台上制造的器件在1550 - 1600纳米范围内表现出低于0.1分贝的附加损耗，1580纳米附近的最小值为0.04分贝，775纳米处的最小值为0.021分贝。结合片上量子状态生成、低损耗干涉仪和检测方面的最新进展，这些结果使TFLN平台上的高保真量子光电路成为可能。


### Abstract

Thin-film lithium niobate (TFLN) has emerged as a leading platform for large-scale programmable photonic circuits for quantum and classical applications. As circuits scale in complexity, low-loss routing of broadband pump and signal fields becomes essential. Here, we present closed-form analytical models and experimentally demonstrate compact, fast-quasi-adiabatic driving-optimized wavelength combiners and filters operating at the fundamental harmonic (FH, 1550 nm) and second-harmonic (SH, 775 nm) wavelengths. Our designs achieve ultra-low loss below 0.06 dB across a 90 nm bandwidth at FH, while maintaining extinction ratios exceeding 25 dB. At SH, the loss remains below 0.12 dB over a 45 nm bandwidth with extinction ratios greater than 19 dB. Devices fabricated on a 300-nm TFLN platform exhibit added loss below 0.1 dB across 1550 - 1600 nm, with minimum values of 0.04 dB around 1580 nm and 0.021 dB at 775 nm. Combined with recent advances in on-chip quantum state generation, low-loss interferometers, and detection, these results enable high-fidelity quantum photonic circuits on the TFLN platform.

## 将Julia-ITensors集成到张量网络量子虚拟机（TNQVD）中

**Original Title:** Integrating Julia-ITensors into the Tensor Network Quantum Virtual Machine (TNQVM)

**Authors:** Zachary W. Windom, Daniel Claudino, Vicente Leyton-Ortega

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27037v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.27037v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-27


### 摘要

张量网络量子虚拟机（TNQVC）是一款针对极限规模ACencialator（XACC）框架的高性能经典电路模拟后台，该框架利用智能张量（ITensor）库进行基于张量网络的量子电路模拟。然而，TNQVR最初的C++ ITensor后台与较旧的集成版本绑定，从而限制了对积极开发的基于Julia的ITensors生态系统中可用的更新张量网络算法、诊断和性能改进的访问。我们引入了JuliaITensorTNQVM，这是一个互操作层，通过C兼容的应用程序二进制接口将TNQVM的C++访问者基础设施和Julia-ITensors运行时连接起来。该设计保留了现有的XACC/TNQPM编程模型，同时能够访问现代张量网络功能，包括直接暴露给XACC的纠缠量信息。我们通过两项研究评估了实现：使用哈尔随机状态的页面曲线验证协议，以及3-正规图上的QAOA MaxCut模拟。在这些测试的机制中，结果与预期的纠缠行为和既定的缩放趋势一致，支持JuliaITensorTNQVMs作为TNQVM中张量网络模拟的实用现代化路径。


### Abstract

The Tensor Network Quantum Virtual Machine (TNQVM) is a high-performance classical circuit simulation backend for the eXtreme-scale ACCelerator (XACC) framework that leverages the Intelligent Tensor (ITensor) library for tensor network--based quantum circuit simulation. However, TNQVM's original C++ ITensor backend is tied to an older integrated release, limiting access to newer tensor network algorithms, diagnostics, and performance improvements available in the actively developed Julia-based ITensors ecosystem. We introduce JuliaITensorTNQVM, an interoperability layer that bridges TNQVM's C++ visitor infrastructure and the Julia-ITensors runtime through a C-compatible application binary interface. This design preserves the existing XACC/TNQVM programming model while enabling access to modern tensor network capabilities, including entanglement entropy diagnostics exposed directly to XACC. We evaluate the implementation through two studies: a Page-curve verification protocol using Haar-random states, and QAOA MaxCut simulations on 3-regular graphs. Within these tested regimes, results are consistent with expected entanglement behavior and established scaling trends, supporting JuliaITensorTNQVM as a practical modernization path for tensor network simulation in TNQVM.

## 从基本原理推导薛定汉方程

**Original Title:** Derivation of the Schrodinger equation from fundamental principles

**Authors:** Wenzhuo Zhang, Anatoly Svidzinsky

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27041v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.27041v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-27


### 摘要

薛定谔通往量子力学波动方程的道路是启发式的，更多地是由物理直觉而不是形式推导来指导的。在这里，我们推导出粒子波函数的薛定谔方程，假设它具有在时间t在点r处找到粒子的概率振幅的意义，并且关系式E=hw，p=hk用相关概率波的频率和波矢来表示粒子的能量和动量。


### Abstract

Schrodinger path to the quantum mechanical wave equation was heuristic and guided more by physical intuition than formal deduction. Here we derive the Schrodinger equation for the particle wave function, assuming that it has a meaning of the probability amplitude to find the particle at time t at point r and the relations E=hw, p=hk expressing particle energy and momentum in terms of the frequency and wave vector of the associated probability wave.


---


## 量子分层细胞神经网络中的模式形成

**Original Title:** Pattern Formation in Quantum Hierarchical Cellular Neural Networks

**Authors:** W. A. Zúñiga-Galindo, B. A. Zambrano-Luna, Chayapuntika Indoung

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27063v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.27063v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-28


### 摘要

我们提出了一类新的量子神经网络（QNN），其状态是$p$-adic Schrödinger方程的解，该方程具有控制神经元之间相互作用的非局部势。这些方程是通过$p$-adic细胞神经网络（CNN）状态方程的威克旋转获得的。CNN是离散分层神经网络（NN）的连续极限。CNN受到威尔逊-考恩模型的生物启发，该模型描述了大量神经元的宏观动力学。我们提供了一个详细的研究新的p$-adic薛定谔方程的离散化，它允许新的QNN简单的图形上的建设。我们还进行了详细的数值模拟，为新QNN的功能提供了清晰的见解。在一个数学水平上，我们证明了新的p$adic薛定谔方程的局部解的存在性。


### Abstract

We present a new class of quantum neural networks (QNNs) whose states are solutions of $p$-adic Schrödinger equations with a non-local potential that controls the interaction between the neurons. These equations are obtained as Wick rotations of the state equations of $p$-adic cellular neural networks (CNNs). The CNNs are continuous limits of discrete hierarchical neural networks (NNs). The CNNs are bio-inspired in the Wilson-Cowan model, which describes the macroscopic dynamics of large populations of neurons. We provide a detailed study of the discretization of the new $p$-adic Schrödinger equations, which allows the construction of new QNNs on simple graphs. We also conduct detailed numerical simulations, offering a clear insight into the functioning of the new QNNs. At a mathematical level, we show the existence of local solutions for the new $p$ -adic Schrödinger equations.

## 具有量子增强光模临界压缩态的信号场幅度估计

**Original Title:** Quantum-enhanced estimation of signal field amplitudes with critical squeezed states of photonic modes

**Authors:** Ken Chen, Jia-Hao Lv, Wen Ning, Zhen-Biao Yang, Shi-Biao Zheng

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27100v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.27100v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-28


### 摘要

量子系统的临界现象为提高测量精度提供了一种很有前途的策略。迄今为止，利用量子比特与光场相互作用的复合系统的量子演化态，已经提出了许多临界增强的量子纠缠方案。这些方案侧重于测量系统的固有频率。本文提出了一种临界增强的量子传感方案，旨在利用相互作用的量子比特-光子系统来估计外部信号场的幅度。信号场与光模耦合，因此复合系统具有独特的暗状态，其中光模遵循压缩真空状态。有关信号场幅度的信息被编码在量子化的光模的一个四分之一中，该光模在临界点附近表现出分歧行为。相对于编码信号的时间和场模式的量子数，测量精度可以接近海森堡极限。


### Abstract

Critical phenomena of quantum systems offer a promising strategy to improve measurement precision. So far, many criticality-enhanced quantum metrological schemes have been proposed by using the adiabatically evolved photonic states of composite systems involving a qubit and a field interacting with each other. These schemes focus on the measurement of the system's inherent frequencies. We here propose a criticality-enhanced quantum sensing protocol, aiming to estimate the amplitude of an external signal field with the interacting qubit-photon system. The signal field is coupled to the photonic mode, so that the composite system has a unique dark state, where the photonic mode follows a squeezed vacuum state. The information about the signal field amplitude is encoded in one quadrature of the quantized photonic mode, which exhibits a divergent behavior near the critical point. The measurement precision can approach the Heisenberg limit with respect to the time to encode the signal and the photon number of the field mode.

## 量子Rabi模型中的非经典光团关联

**Original Title:** Nonclassical Photon-Bundle Correlations in Quantum Rabi Models

**Authors:** Yong-Xin Zhang, Chen Wang, Qing-Hu Chen

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27160v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.27160v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-28


### 摘要

我们使用量子修饰主方程研究了量子Rabi模型及其扩展情况中的非经典光束相关性。通过调节有限温度下的光-物质耦合强度，量子Rabi模型在双量子束聚束和反聚束之间表现出可控的非经典转变，从而允许双量子束发射和统计。我们进一步引入各向异性耦合和非线性斯塔克相互作用，这丰富了量子统计行为并提供了光束相关性的额外可调性。研究发现极端相关行为与激发态量子相转变密切相关，这表明了预测和利用激发态现象的潜在途径。这些效应可以仅通过调节固有系统参数来控制，而不需要外部调制场。因此，量子Rabi模型家族为高纯度量子束产生和可控多量子源提供了一个灵活且实验上可行的平台。


### Abstract

We investigate nonclassical photon-bundle correlations in the quantum Rabi model and its extended cases, using the quantum dressed master equation. By tuning the light--matter coupling strength at finite temperature, the quantum Rabi model exhibits controllable nonclassical transitions between two-photon bundle bunching and antibunching, allowing for the two-photon bundle emission and statistics. We further introduce anisotropic coupling and nonlinear Stark interactions, which enrich the photon statistical behaviors and provide additional tunability of photon-bundle correlations. Extreme correlation behaviors are found to be closely linked to excited-state quantum phase transitions, suggesting a potential pathway for predicting and exploiting excited-state phenomena. These effects can be controlled solely by tuning intrinsic system parameters, without the need for an external modulating field. The quantum Rabi model family thus provides a flexible and experimentally feasible platform for high-purity photon bundle generation and controllable multi-photon sources.

## 量子重力地磁相互作用

**Original Title:** Quantum gravitodiamagnetic interaction

**Authors:** Di Hao, Jiawei Hu, Hongwei Yu

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27180v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.27180v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-28


### 摘要

在线性化量子引力的框架下，我们研究了两个大质量物体的引力磁耦合与引力场的真空涨落引起的量子引力相互作用。从引力场中粒子的拉格朗日量出发，采用韦尔重力电磁学的形式主义，我们推导出与重力磁耦合相关的相互作用Hamilton。与重电和重磁相互作用中出现的线性耦合不同，重磁耦合二次依赖于重磁场。基于这个Hamilton量，我们表明，对于处于底价的球对称引力类氢系统，诱导的四极矩与所施加的重力磁场具有相反的符号，而所施加的重力磁场是重力磁的定义特征。使用首阶微扰理论，我们进一步获得了所产生的相互作用势的显式表达，该表达是有吸引力的，并且在所有距离下均为$r^{-11}$，其中$r$表示两个物体之间的距离。


### Abstract

In the framework of linearized quantum gravity, we investigate the quantum gravitational interaction induced by the gravitodiamagnetic coupling of two massive objects to vacuum fluctuations of the gravitational field. Starting from the Lagrangian of a particle in a gravitational field and employing the formalism of Weyl gravitoelectromagnetism, we derive the interaction Hamiltonian associated with gravitodiamagnetic coupling. Unlike the linear couplings that arise in gravitoelectric and gravitomagnetic interactions, the gravitodiamagnetic coupling depends quadratically on the gravitomagnetic field. Based on this Hamiltonian, we show that, for a spherically symmetric gravitational hydrogen-like system in its ground state, the induced quadrupole moment has the opposite sign to the applied gravitomagnetic field, which is the defining signature of gravitodiamagnetism. Using leading-order perturbation theory, we further obtain an explicit expression for the resulting interaction potential, which is attractive and scales as $r^{-11}$ at all separations, where $r$ denotes the distance between the two objects.

## 在毫克尔文温度下使用AQFP逻辑的超低功耗一致量子位控制

**Original Title:** Ultralow-power coherent qubit control using AQFP logic at millikelvin temperatures

**Authors:** Hiroto Mukai, Akiyoshi Tomonaga, Rui Wang, Yu Zhou, Taro Yamashita, Nobuyuki Yoshikawa, Jaw-Shen Tsai, Naoki Takeuchi

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27231v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.27231v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-28


### 摘要

量子位控制器对于扩展超导量子处理器至关重要，但由于严格的冷却限制，在稀释冰箱的10 mK级实施它们仍然具有挑战性。在这里，我们报告了一种使用隔热量子通量参数（AQFP）逻辑的超低功耗量子位控制器，称为具有虚拟Z门的AQFP多路传输量子位控制器（AQFP QC-VZ）。AQFP QC-VZ生成多音微波脉冲用于量子位控制，具有每个量子位111 pW的超低功耗。通过结合微波和时分多路传输，AQFP QC-VZ仅使用室温下的几条控制线即可将X门和虚拟Z门并行应用于多个量子位。我们使用AQFP混合器（AQFP QC-VZ的核心组件）在10 mK级演示了相干单量子位门，没有明显的一致性下降。


### Abstract

Qubit controllers are essential for scaling superconducting quantum processors, but implementing them at the 10 mK stage of a dilution refrigerator remains challenging due to stringent cooling constraints. Here we report an ultralow-power qubit controller using adiabatic quantum-flux-parametron (AQFP) logic, termed an AQFP-multiplexed qubit controller with virtual Z gates (AQFP QC-VZ). The AQFP QC-VZ generates multi-tone microwave pulses for qubit control with an ultralow power dissipation of 111 pW per qubit. By combining microwave and time-division multiplexing, the AQFP QC-VZ enables parallel application of X and virtual Z gates to multiple qubits using only a few control lines from room temperature. We demonstrate coherent single-qubit gates at the 10 mK stage using an AQFP mixer, a core component of the AQFP QC-VZ, without observable degradation in coherence.

## 从基础心电图模型到NISQ学习者：将心电图创始人提炼成VQC学生

**Original Title:** From Foundation ECG Models to NISQ Learners: Distilling ECGFounder into a VQC Student

**Authors:** Giovanni dos Santos Franco, Felipe Mahlow, Ellison Fernando Cardoso, Felipe Fanchini

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27269v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.27269v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-28


### 摘要

基础模型最近改进了心电图（心电图）表示学习，但它们的部署可能会受到计算成本和延迟限制的限制。在这项工作中，我们将ECGFounder微调为PTB-XL和MIT-BIH心律失常数据库上二元心电图分类的高容量教师，并研究知识蒸馏是否可以将其预测行为转移到紧凑的学生。我们评估了两个经典的1D学生（ResNet-1D和轻量级CNN-1D）和一个量子就绪管道，该管道结合了卷积自动编码器（将256个样本的心电图窗口压缩为低维潜在表示）与6量子位量子变分电路在QisKit中实现并在模拟后台执行。在这两个数据集中，教师提供了最强的整体表现，而蒸馏在可训练参数大幅减少的情况下培养出有竞争力的学生。我们进一步分析了学生表现对蒸馏设置的敏感性，强调了在统一评估协议下将基础心电图模型压缩为经典和量子准备学习器时一致的准确性--效率权衡。


### Abstract

Foundation models have recently improved electrocardiogram (ECG) representation learning, but their deployment can be limited by computational cost and latency constraints. In this work, we fine-tune ECGFounder as a high-capacity teacher for binary ECG classification on PTB-XL and the MIT-BIH Arrhythmia Database, and investigate whether knowledge distillation can transfer its predictive behavior to compact students. We evaluate two classical 1D students (ResNet-1D and a lightweight CNN-1D) and a quantum-ready pipeline that combines a convolutional autoencoder, which compresses 256-sample ECG windows into a low-dimensional latent representation, with a 6-qubit variational quantum circuit implemented in Qiskit and executed in a simulated backend. Across both datasets, the teacher provides the strongest overall performance, while distillation yields competitive students under a considerable reduction in trainable parameters. We further analyze the sensitivity of student performance to distillation settings, highlighting consistent accuracy--efficiency trade-offs when compressing a foundation ECG model into classical and quantum-ready learners under a unified evaluation protocol.

## BB 84量子密钥分发中的量子误比特率分析：测量、统计估计和发射器丢弃检测

**Original Title:** Quantum Bit Error Rate Analysis in BB84 Quantum Key Distribution: Measurement, Statistical Estimation, and Eavesdropping Detection

**Authors:** Jaydeep Rath, Prajwal Panth, P. S. N. Bhaskar

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27278v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.27278v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-28


### 摘要

量子密钥分发（QKD）通过利用量子力学原理提供信息理论安全性。在QKD协议中，BB 84方案仍然是理论研究和实际实现中采用最广泛的方案。决定BB 84可靠性和安全性的一个关键参数是量子误比特率（QBER），它量化了由通道噪音或潜在窃听引起的筛选密钥中的错误。本文对BB 84协议中的QBER进行了系统回顾和分析，研究了其计算、统计估计方法以及在检测窃听活动中的作用。模拟结果经报告的实验观察证实，揭示了窃听强度与QBER之间的近线性关系，在完全拦截-重新发送攻击下，该值接近25%。比较了四种置信区间估计方法Wald、Wilson、Clopper-Pearson和Hoeffding不等式，以在有限关键场景中进行稳健的QBER分析。讨论了包括诱饵状态方法、混合加密模型和抗量子认证在内的协议增强，作为在光纤、自由空间、水下和卫星QKD系统中减轻错误和增强弹性的机制。区分噪音引起的错误与恶意窃听的开放挑战，以及自适应错误纠正和机器学习辅助QBER估计在未来量子网络中的作用，被确定为进一步研究的关键方向。


### Abstract

Quantum Key Distribution (QKD) provides information-theoretic security by exploiting the principles of quantum mechanics. Among QKD protocols, the BB84 scheme remains the most widely adopted for both theoretical research and practical implementation. A critical parameter determining the reliability and security of BB84 is the Quantum Bit Error Rate (QBER), which quantifies errors in the sifted key arising from channel noise or potential eavesdropping. This paper presents a systematic review and analysis of QBER within the BB84 protocol, examining its calculation, statistical estimation methods, and role in detecting eavesdropping activity. Simulation results, corroborated by reported experimental observations, reveal a near-linear relationship between eavesdropping intensity and QBER, with values approaching 25% under full intercept-resend attacks. Four confidence interval estimation methods, Wald, Wilson, Clopper-Pearson, and Hoeffding's inequality, are compared for robust QBER analysis in finite-key scenarios. Protocol enhancements, including decoy-state methods, hybrid cryptographic models, and quantum-resistant authentication, are discussed as mechanisms to mitigate errors and strengthen resilience across fiber, free-space, underwater, and satellite QKD systems. Open challenges in distinguishing noise-induced errors from malicious eavesdropping, and the role of adaptive error correction and machine-learning-assisted QBER estimation in future quantum networks, are identified as key directions for further research.


---


## NNQA：用于端到端多项式综合的神经原生量子算法

**Original Title:** NNQA: Neural-Native Quantum Arithmetic for End-to-End Polynomial Synthesis

**Authors:** Ziqing Guo, Jie Li, Yong Chen, Ziwen Pan

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27297v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.27297v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-28


### 摘要

混合经典量子学习经常受到通用变分分析的通信负担和逼近误差的干扰。在这项研究中，我们引入了神经原生量子算术（NNQA），它将经典学习的非线性表示汇编成由原生么正块组成的精确量子算术。从理论上讲，我们证明了通过将经典神经网络转化为量子电路可以实现量子方程算术的普适逼近，由此产生的误差仅由测量散粒噪音引起，从而将经典的操作员级估计保证扩展到量子区域。对IBM Quantum Heron 3和IonQ Forte处理器的经验验证表明，性能主要受到设备噪音的限制，而没有变化微调：我们对高达35度的多项函数实现了超过99.5%的准确性，并在IonQ硬件上展示了高达36个量子位和70的电路深度的可扩展性，达到可忽略的RSSE 0.005。总体而言，NNQA为原生量子计算建立了一种合成量子算术的新范式。


### Abstract

Hybrid classical quantum learning is often bottlenecked by communication overhead and approximation error from generic variational ansatzes. In this study, we introduce Neural Native Quantum Arithmetic (NNQA), which compiles classically learned nonlinear representations into precise quantum arithmetic composed of native unitary blocks. Theoretically, we prove that the universal approximation of quantum polynomial arithmetic can be realized by transforming a classical neural network into a quantum circuit, with the resulting error arising solely from measurement shot noise, thereby extending classical operator-level estimation guarantees into the quantum regime. Empirical validation on IBM Quantum Heron3 and IonQ Forte processors shows performance limited primarily by device noise without variational fine tuning: we achieve over 99.5% accuracy for polynomials up to degree 35 and demonstrate scalability on IonQ hardware up to 36 qubits and circuit depths of 70, reaching a negligible RMSE of 0.005. Overall, NNQA establishes a new paradigm of synthesizing quantum arithmetic for native quantum computation.

## 环上的到达时间和相对论量子钟

**Original Title:** Time of arrival on a ring and relativistic quantum clocks

**Authors:** Iason Vakondios, Charis Anastopoulos

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27311v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.27311v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-28


### 摘要

我们研究了被限制在环上移动的相对论粒子的到达时间问题，完全在量子场论（QFT）内阐述了该问题。与直线运动的对应结构相反，圆布局意味着粒子在检测之前可能会多次遇到检测器，因此对测量相互作用进行场论处理至关重要。我们采用量子时间概率（QTP）方法直接从QFT中推导出到达时间可观测量的一类正操作值测量（POVMs）。我们分析了半经典和全量子体系中产生的检测概率，确定了相关的时间尺度及其对场论参数的依赖性。对于粒子集合来说，检测信号是一个周期函数，提供了量子时钟的实现，其操作反映了局部时空结构。我们还将形式主义扩展到旋转环，并表明旋转会在检测概率中引发额外的噪音，可以解释为旋转昂鲁效应的表现。最后，我们研究了多时间测量，并证明了由于纠缠而出现的非经典时间相关性。


### Abstract

We study the time-of-arrival problem for relativistic particles constrained to move on a ring, formulating the problem entirely within Quantum Field Theory (QFT). In contrast to its counterpart for motion in a line, the circle topology implies that particles may encounter the detector multiple times before detection, making a field-theoretic treatment of the measurement interaction essential. We employ the Quantum Temporal Probabilities (QTP) method to derive a class of Positive-Operator-Valued Measures (POVMs) for time-of-arrival observables directly from QFT. We analyze the resulting detection probabilities in both semiclassical and fully quantum regimes, identifying the relevant timescales and their dependence on the field-theoretic parameters. For ensembles of particles, the detection signal is a periodic function, providing a realization of a quantum clock whose operation reflects the local spacetime structure. We also extend the formalism to rotating rings and show that rotation induces additional noise in detection probabilities, interpretable as a manifestation of the rotational Unruh effect. Finally, we investigate multi-time measurements and demonstrate the emergence of non-classical temporal correlations due to entanglement.


---


## 单量子增强I型融合门

**Original Title:** Single-photon-boosted type-I fusion gates

**Authors:** A. A. Melkozerov, S. S. Straupe, M. Yu. Saygin

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27315v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.27315v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-28


### 摘要

聚变测量是线性光学量子计算和量子网络的关键基础。I型和II型融合门广泛用于将小型纠缠资源状态组合为更大的光状态，但如果没有辅助资源，它们的成功概率仅限于1/2美元。现有的3/4美元高效I型方案依赖于纠缠Bell对辅助状态，其准备本身就是概率性和资源密集型的。在这里，我们提出了一种增强型I型融合门，仅使用四个辅助单量子和无源线性光学器件即可实现3/4美元的总成功概率。门直接成功的可能性为5/8美元，而蒸馏步骤将部分纠缠的结果转化为额外的成功事件。我们通过估计产生代表性大型纠缠光态所需的光资源来量化该方案的实际优势，并表明提出的门显着减少了所需的费用。这些结果扩展了资源高效的线性光学基元集，并大幅降低了可扩展的光量子计算和量子通信的资源需求。


### Abstract

Fusion measurements are a key primitive for linear-optical quantum computing and quantum networks. Type-I and type-II fusion gates are widely used to combine small entangled resource states into larger photonic states, but without ancillary resources their success probability is limited to $1/2$. Existing $3/4$-efficient type-I schemes rely on entangled Bell-pair ancillary states, whose preparation is itself probabilistic and resource-intensive. Here we propose a boosted type-I fusion gate that achieves a total success probability of $3/4$ using only four ancillary single photons and passive linear optics. The gate succeeds directly with probability $5/8$, while a distillation step converts partially entangled outcomes into additional successful events. We quantify the practical advantage of this scheme by estimating the photonic resources required for generating representative large entangled photonic states and show that the proposed gate significantly reduces the required overhead. These results expand the set of resource-efficient linear-optical primitives and enable a substantial reduction in the resource requirements for scalable photonic quantum computing and quantum communication.


---


## 量子霍尔态对环形几何变形的响应

**Original Title:** Quantum Hall States response to toroidal geometry deformation

**Authors:** Bruno Mera, José M. Mourão, João P. Nunes, Carolina Paiva

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27319v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.27319v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-28


### 摘要

本文应用几何量子化技术研究了量子霍尔效应和分数量子霍尔效应对环形几何变形的响应。主要方法是使用复时间Hamilton演化来诱导几何变化，然后通过相关的广义相干态变换（gCST）来寻找Laughlin状态的演化。我们考虑两种变形。第一种是扁平环形变形。尽管之前已经彻底研究过所有扁平环形几何体的劳克林状态，但我们相信我们通过gCST的方法是新颖的。它还充当研究非平坦凯勒变形的试验场。平坦变形中使用的Hamilton在平移生成元中是二次的，因此是非周期性的。第二种变形涉及非平坦凯勒环形变形，由环面上的全局（即双周期）Hamilton体产生。相应的虚时间流是（椭圆曲线模）$T $-环上凯勒度量空间中的保持Mabuchi测地线，在有限虚时间中遇到弯曲奇异性。通过限制在$S ' 1 $-不变变形，我们找到了环形几何和劳克林状态一直到奇异性的演变的显式解析表达。


### Abstract

In this paper, we apply techniques of geometric quantization to study the response of the integer and fractional quantum Hall effects to toroidal geometry deformation. The main method is that of using complex time Hamiltonian evolution to induce the geometry change and then the associated generalized coherent state transforms (gCST) to find the evolution of the Laughlin states. We consider two kinds of deformations. The first are flat toroidal deformations. Although Laughlin states for all flat toroidal geometries have been thoroughly studied before, we believe that our approach via the gCST is novel. It also serves as a testing ground to study the non-flat Kähler deformations. The Hamiltonians used in the flat deformations are quadratic in the generators of translations and therefore non periodic. The second kind of deformations involve nonflat Kähler toroidal deformations, generated by global, thus bi-periodic, Hamiltonians on the torus. The corresponding imaginary time flows are (elliptic curve modulus) $τ$-preserving Mabuchi geodesics in the space of Kähler metrics on the torus, hitting a curvature singularity in finite imaginary time. By restricting to $S^1$-invariant deformations we find explicit analytic expressions for the evolution of the toroidal geometry and of the Laughlin states all the way to the singularity.


---


## 量子条件随机过程

**Original Title:** Quantum Conditional Stochastic Processes

**Authors:** Stan Gudder

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27369v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.27369v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-28


### 摘要

量子力学包含一些奇怪的非物理概念。其中包括复数、具有其正和自伴运算符的Hilbert空间、由复载体表示的状态、状态的叠加、波函数的坍缩、概率的博恩规则等。如果我们接受量子力学是概率的，那么这些概念就可以被推导出来，并且它们就成为次要的。在这项工作中，我们从所谓的\textit{条件随机过程}（MPS）开始，它基于真实数字和概率。正如我们将要看到的那样，此类过程由三个简单的公理定义。然后，我们通过使用称为\textit{dictionary}的对应关系来使用CPS来推导量子力学。我们还表明反之亦然。也就是说，从量子系统开始，我们使用字典来推导出一个MPS。


### Abstract

Quantum mechanics contains some strange unphysical concepts. Among these are complex numbers, Hilbert spaces with their unitary and self-adjoint operators, states represented by complex vectors, superpositions of states, collapse of wave functions, Born's rule for probabilities and others. If we accept that quantum mechanics is probabilistic, then these concepts can be derived and they become secondary. In this work, we begin with what we call a \textit{conditional stochastic process} (CSP) which is based on real numbers and probabilities. As we shall see, such processes are defined by three simple axioms. We then use CSP to derive quantum mechanics by employing a correspondence called a \textit{dictionary}. We also show that the converse holds. That is, beginning with a quantum system, we employ the dictionary to derive a CSP.


---


## 非元元量子机器学习：Fisher效率从分布式量子表现性转变

**Original Title:** Non-Unitary Quantum Machine Learning: Fisher Efficiency Transitions from Distributed Quantum Expressivity

**Authors:** Apoorv Kumar Masta, Srinjoy Ganguly, Shalini Devendrababu, Farina Riaz, Rajib Rana, Björn Schuller

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27377v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.27377v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-28


### 摘要

与经典方法相比，量子机器学习因其实际优势而面临越来越多的审查，特别是在去量化结果和挑战早期乐观主张的大规模基准研究之后。这项工作对通过混合量子经典神经网络中的一元线性组合框架实施的非一元量子机器学习进行了系统的实证评估。在跨越四个领域的570多项实验中，数字分类MNIST、农业疾病检测PlantVillage、分子性质回归QM 9和医学组织病理学PathMNIST非单位量子层以结构相同的单位基线为基准。在所有领域中都观察到一致的性能改进，根据数据集复杂性和量子位计数，提高幅度从+0.2%到+5.8%不等。一个特别值得注意的发现是医学成像任务中的Fisher效率转变，随着量子位计数从10增加到12，参数效率从负变为正，这表明依赖阈值的效率机制。此外，非单位IQP电路变体在CIFAR 10上的10个量子位处达到或超过经典基线，这表明具有既定复杂性理论硬度保证的电路仍然与LCU框架下的竞争学习性能兼容。这些结果提供了一个大规模、基于证据的条件描述，在这些条件下，非单位QML在短期环境中产生可测量的经验效益。


### Abstract

Quantum machine learning has faced growing scrutiny over its practical advantages compared to classical approaches, particularly following dequantization results and large scale benchmarking studies that have challenged earlier optimistic claims. This work presents a systematic empirical evaluation of non unitary quantum machine learning implemented via the Linear Combination of Unitaries framework within hybrid quantum classical neural networks. Across more than 570 experiments spanning four domains digit classification MNIST, agricultural disease detection PlantVillage, molecular property regression QM9, and medical histopathology PathMNIST non unitary quantum layers are benchmarked against structurally identical unitary baselines. Consistent performance improvements are observed across all domains, with gains ranging from +0.2 percentage to +5.8 percentage depending on dataset complexity and qubit count. A particularly notable finding is a Fisher efficiency transition in medical imaging tasks, where parameter efficiency shifts from negative to positive as qubit count increases from 10 to 12, indicating a threshold dependent efficiency regime. Additionally, non unitary IQP circuit variants reach or exceed classical baselines at 10 qubits on CIFAR 10, demonstrating that circuits with established complexity theoretic hardness guarantees remain compatible with competitive learning performance under the LCU framework. These results offer a large scale, evidence based characterisation of the conditions under which non unitary QML yields measurable empirical benefits in near term settings.


---


## WSee中通过磁垒的旋转谷分辨隧道效应$_2 $

**Original Title:** Spin--valley--resolved tunneling through magnetic barriers in WSe$_2$

**Authors:** Rachid El Aitouni, Clarence Cortes, David Laroze, Ahmed Jellal

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27384v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.27384v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-28


### 摘要

我们研究了磁场对WS $e_2 $电子性质的影响，重点关注旋转轨道耦合、旋转和谷极化以及电导。我们解析地求解特征值方程，并使用连续性方程根据电流密度确定传输概率。我们使用Büttiker公式计算电导率。我们的数字结果表明，通过$K$谷传播的可能性比通过$K '$谷传播的可能性更大。对于这两个山谷，都清楚地观察到克莱因隧道效应。电导率受到磁场增加的影响，因为它通过塞曼效应改变了费米子的能量水平。这些修改使得费米子能够限制在屏障内。旋转和谷极化也受到磁场的影响。随着场强度的增加，它会引导费米子并确定哪个通道可以穿过屏障。这增加了另一个控制费米子的工具，为谷电子学和谷过滤信息存储的相关应用铺平了道路。


### Abstract

We investigate the influence of a magnetic field on the electronic properties of WS$e_2$ with a focus on spin-orbit coupling, spin and valley polarization, and conductance. We solve the eigenvalue equation analytically and use the continuity equation to determine the transmission probability based on current densities. We calculate the conductance using Büttiker formula. Our numerical results indicate that transmission through the $K$ valley is more likely than through the $K'$ valley. For both valleys, the Klein tunneling effect is clearly observed. The conductance is affected by an increase in the magnetic field because it alters the energy levels of fermions via the Zeeman effect. These modifications enable the confinement of fermions within the barrier. Spin and valley polarization are also influenced by the magnetic field. As the field intensity increases, it steers the fermions and determines which channel can cross the barrier. This adds another tool of controlling fermions, paving the way for relevant applications in valleytronics and valley filtering for information storage.


---


## 非马尔科夫退相动力学中的一致性和热性之间的权衡

**Original Title:** Trade-off between coherence and heat in a non-Markovian dephasing dynamics

**Authors:** Marino P. Lenzarini, Diogo O. Soares-Pinto

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27387v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.27387v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-28


### 摘要

量子一致性如何影响热力学行为仍然是量子热力学中的一个悬而未决的问题。在这里，我们在纯去相框架内研究这种关系，其中中心量子位与有限的类伊辛旋转环境相互作用。尽管系统的内能保持不变，但相互作用会引起退散并产生重要的热力学特征。在两点测量方法中，我们表明消散到环境中的热量与重新制定的量子热力学第一定律中出现的相干能量贡献相匹配。数值计算揭示了振荡一致性动力学，其复兴与信息回流和非马尔科夫效应相关，如Breuer-Laine-Piilo测量所量化的那样。我们发现热量和一致性表现出相互交织的时间行为，一致性衰变期间热量消散增强，复兴期间热量减少。这些结果表明，在经历纯去相的有限封闭复合系统中，一致性动力学和热力学量之间存在联系。


### Abstract

How quantum coherence influences thermodynamic behavior remains an open question in quantum thermodynamics. Here we investigate this relation within the pure dephasing framework, where a central qubit interacts with a finite Ising-like spin environment. Although the system's internal energy remains constant, the interaction induces decoherence and gives rise to nontrivial thermodynamic features. Within the two-point measurement approach, we show that the heat dissipated into the environment matches the coherent energy contribution appearing in a reformulated first law of quantum thermodynamics. Numerical calculations reveal oscillatory coherence dynamics, with revivals associated with information backflow and non-Markovian effects, as quantified by the Breuer-Laine-Piilo measure. We find that heat and coherence exhibit intertwined temporal behavior, with enhanced heat dissipation during coherence decay and reduced heat during revivals. These results suggest a connection between coherence dynamics and thermodynamic quantities in finite, closed composite systems undergoing pure dephasing.

## 通过协议对量子计算机进行基准测试--比较超导和离子阱量子技术

**Original Title:** Benchmarking Quantum Computers via Protocols -- Comparing Superconducting and Ion-Trap Quantum Technology

**Authors:** Nitay Mayo, Tal Mor, Yossi Weinstein

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27397v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.27397v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-28


### 摘要

超导和离子阱量子架构在量子计算领域的当前景观中很常见，每种都具有独特的特征和操作限制。理解和测量这些器件的潜在量子性对于评估它们的实际应用准备情况和指导未来的进展和研究至关重要。在早期工作的基础上（Meirom，Mor，Weinstein Arxiv 2505.12441），我们利用了一种适用于通过直接在最佳子芯片上测量“量子性”来比较这两种架构的基准测试策略。不同于现有的指标，我们的方法采用严格的二进制保真度阈值来自经典的限制状态转移。这使我们能够明确地建立指定子区域的量子优势。我们将这种质量保证方法应用于来自这两种技术的行业领先平台。这种比较提供了基于协议的量子优势评估，不仅揭示了每个测试芯片及其子芯片的优点和缺点，而且还为它们的评估提供了共同语言。通过抽象出最终结果中的技术差异，我们展示了一种基准策略，该策略弥合了不同量子电路技术之间的差距，实现公平的性能比较，并为评估未来量子优势主张奠定了重要基础。


### Abstract

Superconducting and Ion-Trap quantum architectures are common in the current landscape of the quantum computing field, each with distinct characteristics and operational constraints. Understanding and measuring the underlying quantumness of these devices is essential for assessing their readiness for practical applications and guiding future progress and research. Building on earlier work (Meirom, Mor, Weinstein Arxiv 2505.12441), we utilize a benchmarking strategy applicable for comparing these two architectures by measuring "quantumness" directly on optimal sub-chips. Distinct from existing metrics, our approach employs rigorous binary fidelity thresholds derived from the classical limits of state transfer. This enable us to definitively establish quantum advantage of a designated sub-region. We apply this quality assurance methodology to industry leading platforms from both technologies. This comparison provides a protocol-based evaluation of quantumness advantage, revealing not only the strengths and weaknesses of each tested chip and its sub-chips but also offering a common language for their assessment. By abstracting away technical differences in the final result, we demonstrate a benchmarking strategy that bridges the gap between disparate quantum-circuit technologies, enabling fair performance comparisons and establishing a critical foundation for evaluating future claims of quantum advantage.


---


## 单人造原子SABER

**Original Title:** Single Artificial Atom SASER

**Authors:** Shtefan V. Sanduleanu, Peter Yu. Shlykov, Alexei N. Bolgar, Daria A. Kalacheva, Julia I. Zotova, Gleb P. Fedorov, Viktor B. Lubsanov, Alexei Yu. Dmitriev, Evgenia S. Alekseeva, Oleg V. Astafiev

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27401v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.27401v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-28


### 摘要

激光是正统量子力学的一种效应，于1955年被发现，并因其基础性而于1964年获得诺贝尔奖。如今，激光器和脉泽通常与电磁波一起工作，并由带有活性媒介的共振器组成--通常是具有粒子数倒置机制的原子系统。令人惊讶的是，即使电磁波被格子的振动取代，从而被音素取代，量子力学仍然有效，即使不是基本粒子。通过实现具有粒子数倒置机制的与原子耦合的声共振器，可以实现声音中的激光效应。在本文中，我们通过利用晶体上的表面声波（AW）共振器与精心设计的三原子量子系统（人工原子）耦合，来演示单个人工原子SABER（受激辐射声放大）作用，其中实现了粒子数倒置。SABER在频率约为3 GHz的超声范围内工作。声电信号通过压电效应和电路元件进行转换;人造原子和输入/输出通过声波进行耦合。我们观察到波的放大及其强烈的自发射，并明显缩小了线宽。系统生成的音素数超过90。


### Abstract

Lasing - an effect of orthodox quantum mechanics - was discovered in 1955 and recognized by the Nobel Prize in 1964 due to its fundamentality. Nowadays, lasers and masers routinely work with electromagnetic waves and consist of a resonator with an active medium - usually a system of atoms with population inversion mechanism. Amazingly, quantum mechanics remains valid even when electromagnetic waves are replaced by vibrations of a crystal lattice, and, therefore, photons by phonons, even though are not fundamental particles. By implementing acoustic resonators coupled to an atom with a mechanism of population inversion, the lasing effect in sound can be achieved. In this paper, we demonstrate the single artificial atom SASER (Sound Amplification by Stimulated Emission of Radiation) action by utilizing a surface acoustic wave (SAW) resonator on quartz coupled to a deliberately designed superconducting three-level quantum system (artificial atom), in which population inversion is realized. The SASER operates in the ultrasound range at a frequency about 3 GHz. Acoustic-to-electric signals are converted via piezo-electric effect and the circuit elements; an artificial atom and input/outputs are coupled via the acoustic waves. We observe amplification of the waves and their strong self-emission with a significant narrowing of the linewidth. The phonon number generated in the system exceeds 90.


---


## 时间反演杨氏干涉仪超分辨参数估计的差分源基编码

**Original Title:** Differential source-basis encoding for superresolved parameter estimation in a time-reversed Young interferometer

**Authors:** Jianming Wen

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27407v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.27407v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-28


### 摘要

我们开发了一种用于时逆杨氏干涉仪中局部参数估计的差异源编码协议，其中源平面不仅用作扫描坐标，还用作可编程测量基础。两个顺序的纯正源模式实现了关于所选工作点的反对称差异探测，将确定性源坐标响应转换为求导梯度传感通道。在局部区域中，差异信号自然地分离为一个干扰梯度项（该项也存在于非干涉式差异传感中）和一个干扰梯度项（该项特定于时间反向杨条纹定律）。这种分解确定了干涉优势的物理起源，并澄清了为什么它依赖于制度而不是普遍存在。使用散粒噪音限制的Poisson模型，我们推导出相应的Fisher信息和Cramér-Rao界限，并将该协议与相同几何形状的格栅采样和匹配的非干涉式差异基线进行比较。代表性的数字示例显示了相对于格栅采样的强大而稳健的收益，而时间反向杨干涉的额外改进取决于参数，但在有利的制度下可能会很大。结果将时间反转的Young几何确定为可编程差异干涉测量的实用简单平台。


### Abstract

We develop a differential source-encoding protocol for local parameter estimation in a time-reversed Young interferometer, where the source plane is used not merely as a scan coordinate but as a programmable measurement basis. Two sequential positive-only source patterns implement an antisymmetric differential probe about a chosen operating point, converting the deterministicc source-coordinate response into a derivative-gradient sensing channel. In the local regime, the differential signal separates naturally into an envelope-gradient term, which is also present in noninterferometric differential sensing, and an interference-gradient term, which is specific to the time-reversed Young fringe law. This decomposition identifies the physical origin of the interferometric advantage and clarifies why it is regime dependent rather than universal. Using a shot-noise-limited Poisson model, we derive the corresponding Fisher information and Cramér--Rao bounds and compare the protocol with raster sampling in the same geometry and with a matched noninterferometric differential baseline. Representative numerical examples show a strong and robust gain over raster sampling, while the additional improvement from the time-reversed Young interference is parameter dependent but can be substantial in favorable regimes. The results establish the time-reversed Young geometry as a practically simple platform for programmable differential interferometric metrology.


---


## 无去散相关量子位和光导体QED中巨分子的手征发射

**Original Title:** Decoherence-Free Qubit and Chiral Emission from a Giant Molecule in Waveguide QED

**Authors:** Yang Wang, Juan José García-Ripoll, Alan C. Santos

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27443v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.27443v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-28


### 摘要

在单导量子电动力学（QED）设备中将退相干保护与定向量子发射相结合仍然是一个悬而未决的挑战。在这里，我们表明，人造巨分子--在多个空间分离的点处耦合到光导体的强相互作用人造原子--实现了两者：完全可操作的无去相干（DF）量子比特和状态相关的手征单量子发射，产生于相同的光干涉机制。RST简化为单个原子的局部激发，通过调制单个原子频率来实现通用单量子位门，读出利用状态相关的手征发射，方向性达到100%，测量误差低至1.2%。单个器件中退散保护和定向发射的共存将巨分子定位为光量子动力学中模块化量子网络的受保护的手征节点。


### Abstract

Combining decoherence protection with directional photon emission in a single waveguide quantum electrodynamics (QED) device remains an open challenge. Here we show that an artificial giant molecule -- strongly interacting artificial atoms coupled to a photonic waveguide at multiple spatially separated points -- achieves both: a fully operational decoherence-free (DF) qubit and state-dependent chiral single-photon emission, arising from the same photon-interference mechanism. Initialization reduces to a local excitation of a single atom, universal single-qubit gates are implemented by modulating a single atomic frequency, and readout exploits state-dependent chiral emission with directionality reaching 100% and low measurement error of 1.2%. The coexistence of decoherence protection and directional emission in a single device positions giant molecules as protected chiral nodes for modular quantum networks in waveguide QED.

## 量子场子循环模式真空涨落的时间-能量不确定性关系

**Original Title:** Time-energy uncertainty relation from subcycle mode vacuum fluctuations of a quantum field

**Authors:** Achintya Sajeendran, Timothy C. Ralph

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27468v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.27468v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-29


### 摘要

时间-能量不确定性关系经常被用作相互作用量子场论中虚拟粒子的启发式解释。然而，由于几个原因，这种解释在仔细审查后就被打破了。尽管量子力学中时间-能量不确定性界限的具体推导和解释已经建立，最著名的是曼德尔维纳和塔姆在1945年建立的，但这些界限与量子场论中的虚粒子概念之间并没有已知的严格联系。在这项工作中，我们使用了一个模型，其中与自由纯量场的子周期模式相关的虚拟激励可以以单位效率转换为理想化的快速切换谐振子Unruh-DeWitt检测器的真实激励。与共激场相耦合。将时间不确定性定义为探测器与场相互作用的有效持续时间，我们表明在深子循环区域中满足时间-能量不确定性关系。我们的结果从时间-能量不确定性原理的角度为量子场论中虚粒子的教科书启发式图像提供了具体的操作意义。


### Abstract

The time-energy uncertainty relation is often invoked as a heuristic explanation for virtual particles in interacting quantum field theories. However, this interpretation breaks down upon closer scrutiny for several reasons. Although concrete derivations and interpretations of time-energy uncertainty bounds in quantum mechanics have been established, most famously by Mandelstam and Tamm in 1945, there is no known rigorous connection between these bounds and the concept of virtual particles in quantum field theory. In this work, we use a model in which virtual excitations associated with subcycle modes of a free scalar field can be converted with unit efficiency into real excitations of an idealized rapidly-switched harmonic-oscillator Unruh-DeWitt detector coupled to the conjugate field. Defining the time uncertainty as the effective duration of the detector-field interaction, we show that a time-energy uncertainty relation is satisfied in the deep subcycle regime. Our results provide concrete operational meaning to the textbook heuristic picture of virtual particles in quantum field theory in terms of the time-energy uncertainty principle.


---


## 宏观量子电动力学的一阶Maxwell算符形式

**Original Title:** First order Maxwell operator formalism for macroscopic quantum electrodynamics

**Authors:** Ishita Agarwal, Ankit Kundu, Christian M. Lange, Jonathan D. Hood

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27475v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.27475v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-29


### 摘要

Standard macroscopic QED is built on the second-order Green's function for the electric field and discards open-system boundary terms. Here we develop a first-order electromagnetic operator approach that retains both $\mathbf{E}$ and $\mathbf{H}$ and keeps those boundary terms, naturally leading to a quantum input-output formalism. We recast Maxwell's equations as an operator equation for the dual field $\mathit{E}$=$[\mathbf{E},\mathbf{H}]^T$, whose first-order Green operator $g$ propagates the electromagnetic state between surfaces. Symmetries of the Maxwell operator under energy and reciprocal inner products yield the propagation formula, Lorentz reciprocity, and a generalized optical theorem, with minimal vector calculus. Quantizing via a Heisenberg-Langevin approach for absorptive, dispersive media yields two independent quantum noise sources: bulk Langevin operators from material absorption and input-output field operators at the boundary. Expressing the interior field in terms of these operators and the Green propagator yields an exact closed commutation relation $[{\mathit{E}},{\mathit{E}}^\dagger]\propto \mathrm{Im}\,g$, consistent with the fluctuation-dissipation theorem. This identity holds even when dielectrics extend to the boundary, as in waveguide input-output problems, and enables quantum input-output descriptions of complex photonic structures where the Green's function is obtained numerically, extending the framework beyond cavities and waveguides.


### Abstract

Standard macroscopic QED is built on the second-order Green's function for the electric field and discards open-system boundary terms. Here we develop a first-order electromagnetic operator approach that retains both $\mathbf{E}$ and $\mathbf{H}$ and keeps those boundary terms, naturally leading to a quantum input-output formalism. We recast Maxwell's equations as an operator equation for the dual field $\mathit{E}$=$[\mathbf{E},\mathbf{H}]^T$, whose first-order Green operator $g$ propagates the electromagnetic state between surfaces. Symmetries of the Maxwell operator under energy and reciprocal inner products yield the propagation formula, Lorentz reciprocity, and a generalized optical theorem, with minimal vector calculus. Quantizing via a Heisenberg-Langevin approach for absorptive, dispersive media yields two independent quantum noise sources: bulk Langevin operators from material absorption and input-output field operators at the boundary. Expressing the interior field in terms of these operators and the Green propagator yields an exact closed commutation relation $[{\mathit{E}},{\mathit{E}}^\dagger]\propto \mathrm{Im}\,g$, consistent with the fluctuation-dissipation theorem. This identity holds even when dielectrics extend to the boundary, as in waveguide input-output problems, and enables quantum input-output descriptions of complex photonic structures where the Green's function is obtained numerically, extending the framework beyond cavities and waveguides.


---


## 双身丧失的非二次玻色子刘维利安的精确对角化

**Original Title:** Exact diagonalization of a non-quadratic bosonic Liouvillian with two-body loss

**Authors:** Masaaki Tokieda

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27480v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.27480v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-29


### 摘要

我们给出了具有双体损失项的非二次玻色子刘维利安的完全对角化。刘维利安被证明是完全可对角化的左右汇合超几何函数，其区别源于超级运算符的非交换性质。由此产生的谱分解产生主方程的通解，扩展了之前的结果。我们进一步研究通过非线性伪模的镜头构建非高斯开放系统模型。


### Abstract

We present the full diagonalization of a non-quadratic bosonic Liouvillian with a two-body loss term. The Liouvillian is shown to be exactly diagonalizable in terms of left and right confluent hypergeometric functions, whose distinction arises from the noncommutative nature of superoperators. The resulting spectral decomposition yields the general solution of the master equation, extending previous results. We further investigate the construction of a non-Gaussian open system model through the lens of nonlinear pseudomodes.


---


## 通过交替双色调窄线冷却在浅时钟神奇镊子中对$##^{171}$ZB原子进行高性能成像

**Original Title:** High performance imaging of $^{171}$Yb atom in shallow clock-magic tweezer by alternating dual-tone narrowline cooling

**Authors:** Yunheung Song, Kangheun Kim, Jeong Ho Han, Seungtaek Oh, Jongchul Mun

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27498v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.27498v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-29


### 摘要

我们展示了在759.4纳米波长的时钟神奇镊子中对$^{171}$ZB单原子进行成像，其保真度和存活率均超过99.9%。我们使用交替双色调窄线成像在镊子中实现更有效的三维冷却，允许在200 $μ$K陷阱深度内进行几毫秒成像，这是时钟神奇镊子中用于成像的典型深度的一半。因此，即使没有重新抽运，高保真度的成像存活率仍然接近99.9%，这可以实现基于亚稳搁置的高性能无损量子位测量。此外，我们的模拟预测，更优化的配置可以进一步减少陷阱深度，从而提高成像性能。浅陷阱中的这种成像能力为更通用的陷阱波长开辟了高性能成像，并为超过1，000个量子位的大规模系统和高度可重复的镊子时钟奠定了基础。


### Abstract

We demonstrate imaging $^{171}$Yb single atoms in clock-magic tweezers of 759.4 nm wavelength, with above 99.9% fidelity and survival. We use alternating dual-tone narrowline imaging for more efficient three-dimensional cooling in tweezers, allowing several-millisecond imaging in 200 $μ$K trap depth, which is half of typical depth used for imaging in clock-magic tweezers. Accordingly, even without repumping, imaging survival is still close to 99.9% with the high fidelity, which can enable high performance nondestructive qubit measurements based on metastable shelving. Moreover, our simulation predicts that more optimal configuration could further reduce the trap depth, as improving the imaging performance. This imaging capability in shallow traps opens high performance imaging for more general trap wavelength, and lays the foundation for large scale systems over 1,000 qubits, and highly repeatable tweezer clocks.

## 巨原子控制的相关函数和光-光相互作用

**Original Title:** Correlation Functions and Photon-Photon Interactions Controlled by a Giant Atom

**Authors:** Yanjin Yue, Rui-Yang Gong, Shengyong Li, Ze-Liang Xiang

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27506v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.27506v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-29


### 摘要

通过通过光在光路中限制来增强原子与光的相互作用，WQED为探索量子光学现象提供了一个强大的平台。在这里，我们研究了从左侧射入与双向导相耦合的巨原子的弱相干脉冲的光散射动力学，重点关注小原子逼近中不存在的效应。使用扩展的输入-输出形式主义，我们计算了相关函数，并表明两个散射过程之间的竞争取决于脉冲宽度与原子寿命之比，从而导致聚束和反聚束之间的时间依赖性切换。此外，调整巨原子的两个耦合点之间累积的相允许在三个不同的区域之间切换量子统计，每个区域都有有限的相带宽。我们还讨论了超导体电路实验的可行性。我们的结果为基于巨原子的光脉冲控制和量子控制中的潜在应用提供了一条途径。


### Abstract

Waveguide quantum electrodynamics (WQED) provides a powerful platform for exploring quantum optical phenomena by enhancing atom-photon interactions through photon confinement in a waveguide. Here we investigate the photon-scattering dynamics of a weak coherent pulse incident from the left on a giant atom coupled to a bidirectional waveguide, focusing on effects absent in the small-atom approximation. Using an extended input-output formalism, we calculate the relevant correlation functions and show that the competition between two scattering processes is governed by the ratio of the pulse width to the atomic lifetime, leading to time-dependent switching between bunching and antibunching. In addition, tuning the phase accumulated between the two coupling points of the giant atom allows the photon statistics to be switched among three distinct regimes, each with a finite phase bandwidth. We also discuss the experimental feasibility in superconducting circuits. Our results provide a route toward giant-atom-based control of photon pulses and potential applications in quantum control.

## 选择磁场下双臂旋转梯中的纠缠转移动力学

**Original Title:** Entanglement Transfer Dynamics in a Two-Leg Spin Ladder Under a Selective Magnetic Field

**Authors:** Soghra Ghanavat, Abbas Sabour, Somayeh Mehrabankar

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27511v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.27511v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-29


### 摘要

我们研究了二元纠缠通过由各向异性海森堡（XXZ型）模型控制的两足旋转1/2阶梯的动态传递，选择性磁场专门应用于中介横档。从最大纠缠的初始横档对开始，我们证明了高保真纠缠转移到末端对（对于N = 3个横档对，F_max = 0.9998），中间横档始终保持有效解纠缠。动力学由两个独立的时间尺度决定：频率欧米茄_fast = 2* squtt（1 + 4d ' 2）J（由局部梯级物理设置，与场无关）的快载体振荡和周期T_slow = 2.37 h/J ' 2（由虚拟梯级间耦合设置，与场相关）的慢传递包封。通过二阶微扰理论，通过两个平行的虚拟路径推导出有效梯级间耦合J_eff = Alpha（d，g）J^2/h。我们系统地研究了磁场强度、Hamilton各向异性和初始状态对传输质量的影响，建立了保真度的全局参数空间图，并证明了在不相关耦合无序下的鲁棒性（对于Delta <= 10%，平均F_max > 0.998）。所有结果都是通过对多达N = 5个梯级对的系统的精确对角化获得的;扩展到更大的系统需要张量网络方法，例如DMRG。与一维链方案相比，阶梯几何形状实现了空间选择性控制机制，该机制可以抑制中间纠缠，同时保留相干转移，为工程量子通道提供了独特的途径。


### Abstract

We investigate the dynamical transfer of bipartite entanglement through a two-leg spin-1/2 ladder governed by the anisotropic Heisenberg (XXZ-type) model with a selective magnetic field applied exclusively to the mediating rungs. Starting from a maximally entangled initial rung pair, we demonstrate high-fidelity entanglement transfer to the terminal pair (F_max = 0.9998 for N = 3 rung pairs), with the intermediate rungs remaining effectively disentangled throughout. The dynamics is governed by two independent timescales: a fast carrier oscillation at frequency omega_fast = 2*sqrt(1 + 4d^2) J (set by local rung physics, field-independent) and a slow transfer envelope with period T_slow = 2.37 h/J^2 (set by virtual inter-rung coupling, field-dependent). The effective inter-rung coupling J_eff = alpha(d,g) J^2/h is derived via second-order perturbation theory through two parallel virtual paths. We systematically study the effects of magnetic field strength, Hamiltonian anisotropy, and initial state on transfer quality, establish a global parameter space map of the fidelity, and demonstrate robustness under uncorrelated coupling disorder (mean F_max > 0.998 for delta <= 10%). All results are obtained by exact diagonalisation for systems of up to N = 5 rung pairs; extension to larger systems requires tensor-network methods such as DMRG. Compared to one-dimensional chain proposals, the ladder geometry enables a spatially selective control mechanism that suppresses intermediate entanglement while preserving coherent transfer, providing a distinct route to engineered quantum channels.


---


## 参数化量子电路中的相转变

**Original Title:** Phase transitions in parametrized quantum circuits

**Authors:** Xiaoyang Wang, Han Xu, Lukas Broers, Tomonori Shirakawa, Seiji Yunoki

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27532v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.27532v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-29


### 摘要

相转变是物理系统中最有趣的现象之一，但使用经典算法研究它们接近临界状态的行为仍然具有挑战性。参数化量子电路（PQC）为在实际量子计算机上研究此类机制提供了一种有希望的方法。然而，为了使用它来探测关键行为，PQC本身应该是非平凡的，并表现出相转变和非分析性--这是一种尚未被明确识别的属性。在这项工作中，我们确定了PQC中本质上产生非分析性的机制。作为具体实现，我们构造了一类顺序PQC，其可观测期望值是无限体积极限下电路参数的非解析函数，表明所准备的PQC状态在非解析点发生了相转变。纠缠和确定的序参数在不同的阶段有不同的行为，揭示了PQC状态的相图。我们表明，基于张量网络和泡利传播的PQC的经典模拟在相转变点附近效率较低，这表明使用具有相转变的PQC实现实际量子优势的物理动机途径。


### Abstract

Phase transitions are among the most intriguing phenomena in physical systems, yet their behavior near criticality remain challenging to study using classical algorithms. Parameterized quantum circuits (PQCs) offer a promising approach to investigating such regimes on practical quantum computers. However, in order to use it to probe critical behavior, a PQC itself should be non-trivial and exhibit a phase transition and non-analyticity -- a property that has not yet been clearly identified. In this work, we identify a mechanism for generating non-analyticities intrinsically in PQCs. As a concrete realization, we construct a class of sequential PQCs whose observable expectation value is a non-analytic function of the circuit parameter in the infinite volume limit, showing that the prepared PQC states undergo a phase transition at the non-analytic points. The entanglement and the identified order parameter have distinct behaviors in different phases, revealing a phase diagram of the PQC state. We show that classical simulation of this PQC based on tensor networks and Pauli propagation gets less efficient in the vicinity of the phase transition point, indicating a physically motivated route towards practical quantum advantage using PQCs with phase transitions.


---


## 量子网络中多方纠缠的非同步路由

**Original Title:** Asynchronous Routing for Multipartite Entanglement in Quantum Networks

**Authors:** Chenliang Tian, Zebo Yang, Raj Jain, Ramana Kompella, Reza Nejabati, Eneet Kaur, Aiman Erbad, Mounir Hamdi, Mohamed Abdallah

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27551v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.27551v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-29


### 摘要

在量子网络中，通信的一种方式是通过中间节点的交换来分配纠缠。大多数现有工作主要旨在创建有效的长距离双方端到端纠缠。然而，某些场景还需要用于量子秘密共享和多方计算等应用的远程多方纠缠。我们之前的研究使用一种仅依赖于纠缠链路的本地知识的同步、基于树的路由方案来提高端到端纠缠率，从而节省未使用的纠缠并避免同步操作。本文将这种方法扩展到多方纠缠，特别是格林伯格-霍恩-蔡林格（GZZ）三党国家。它表明，我们的同步协议在纠缠率方面优于传统的同步方法，特别是随着相关时间的增加。这种方法还可以扩展到四方和更大的多方GHZ国家，突出了跨各种网络布局的多方场景的同步路由的有效性和适应性。


### Abstract

In quantum networks, one way to communicate is to distribute entanglements through swapping at intermediate nodes. Most existing work primarily aims to create efficient two-party end-to-end entanglement over long distances. However, some scenarios also require remote multipartite entanglement for applications such as quantum secret sharing and multi-party computation. Our previous study improved end-to-end entanglement rates using an asynchronous, tree-based routing scheme that relies solely on local knowledge of entanglement links, conserving unused entanglement and avoiding synchronous operations. This article extends this approach to multipartite entanglements, particularly the three-party Greenberger-Horne-Zeilinger (GHZ) states. It shows that our asynchronous protocol outperforms traditional synchronous methods in entanglement rates, especially as coherence times increase. This approach can also be extended to four-party and larger multipartite GHZ states, highlighting the effectiveness and adaptability of asynchronous routing for multipartite scenarios across various network topologies.


---


## RADAR-Q：用于多租户量子网络中纠缠分布的资源感知分布式同步路由

**Original Title:** RADAR-Q: Resource-Aware Distributed Asynchronous Routing for Entanglement Distribution in Multi-Tenant Quantum Networks

**Authors:** Chenliang Tian, Zebo Yang, Raj Jain, Ramana Kompella, Reza Nejabati, Eneet Kaur, Aiman Erbad, Mohamed Abdallah, Mounir Hamdi

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27570v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.27570v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-29


### 摘要

可扩展量子网络必须支持并发纠缠请求，但当用户竞争共享转发器资源时，现有的路由协议就会失败，从而浪费脆弱的量子状态。本文提出了RADAR-Q，这是一种资源感知的去中心化路由协议，将实时资源竞争嵌入到路径选择中。与需要全局协调或中央锚点的先前设计不同，RADAR-Q做出智能本地决策，平衡路径长度和保真度、瞬时量子存储器可用性和中间贝尔状态测量（BSM）操作。通过识别DODAQ层次结构中的最近共同祖先（NCA），RADAR-Q将纠缠交换本地化在通信用户附近，避免不必要的中心绕道并减少BSM链长度和去相干暴露。我们根据同步和以根为中心的同步基线在网格和随机拓扑上评估RADAR-Q。结果显示，RADAR-Q的总吞吐量分别比同步和以根为中心的设计高出2.5倍和7.6倍。虽然基线在高负载下遭受灾难性的保真度崩溃至0.5阈值以下，但RADAR-Q始终将端到端保真度保持在0.76以上，确保对保持可用。此外，RADAR-Q表现出近乎完美的公平性（Jain的公平性指数96-98%），并在严格的1.0 ms相关时间下保持了理想吞吐量的50%以上。这些发现将竞争感知的去中心化路由确立为多租户量子网络的可扩展基础。


### Abstract

Scalable quantum networks must support concurrent entanglement requests, yet existing routing protocols fail when users compete for shared repeater resources, wasting fragile quantum states. This paper presents RADAR-Q, a resource-aware decentralized routing protocol embedding real-time resource contention into path selection. Unlike prior designs requiring global coordination or central anchors, RADAR-Q makes intelligent local decisions balancing path length and fidelity, instantaneous quantum memory availability, and intermediate Bell-State Measurement (BSM) operations. By identifying the Nearest Common Ancestor (NCA) within a DODAG hierarchy, RADAR-Q localizes entanglement swapping close to communicating users - avoiding unnecessary central detours and reducing BSM chain length and decoherence exposure. We evaluate RADAR-Q on grid and random topologies against synchronous and root-centric asynchronous baselines. Results show RADAR-Q achieves aggregate throughputs 2.5x and 7.6x higher than synchronized and root-centric designs, respectively. While baselines suffer catastrophic fidelity collapse below the 0.5 threshold under high load, RADAR-Q consistently maintains end-to-end fidelity above 0.76, ensuring pairs remain usable. Furthermore, RADAR-Q exhibits near-perfect fairness (Jain's Fairness Index 96-98%) and retains over 50% of its ideal throughput under stringent 1.0 ms coherence times. These findings establish contention-aware decentralized routing as a scalable foundation for multi-tenant quantum networks.


---


## 利用斯托克斯反斯托克斯相关性的量子控制和信号增强

**Original Title:** Quantum control and signal enhancement exploiting the Stokes-anti-Stokes coherence

**Authors:** Wen-Zhao Zhang, Keye Zhang, Jie Li

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27607v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.27607v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-29


### 摘要

我们提出了斯托克斯和反斯托克斯散射过程之间的相干耦合的理论框架，揭示了任何一个过程单独无法实现的干涉现象。在超出分解边带限制的分散相互作用模型中，我们表明经典驱动和系统带宽将两个通道连贯地链接起来，从而实现了相控干扰。破坏性干涉在分散耦合系统中引起固有的不对称性，从而实现量子信息存储和传输的连贯控制，而相长干涉导致指数信号放大，从而增强量子检测。这项工作为理解斯托克斯反斯托克斯相干性作为量子控制和计量学基础的基本机制建立了统一的图景。此外，它表明，这些功能可以通过实施斯托克斯-反斯托克斯阵列进一步增强。


### Abstract

We present a theoretical framework for the coherent coupling between Stokes and anti-Stokes scattering processes, revealing interference phenomena inaccessible to either process alone. Within a dispersive-interaction model beyond the resolved-sideband limit, we show that classical driving and system linewidth coherently links the two channels, enabling phase-controlled interference. Destructive interference induces intrinsic asymmetry in dispersively coupled systems, enabling coherent control of quantum information storage and transfer, while constructive interference leads to exponential signal amplification and thus enhanced quantum detection. This work establishes a unified picture for understanding Stokes-anti-Stokes coherence as a fundamental mechanism underlying both quantum control and metrology. Furthermore, it suggests that these functionalities can be further enhanced by implementing Stokes-anti-Stokes arrays.


---


## 单个和耦合量子位的共振激发用于相干量子控制和微波检测

**Original Title:** Resonant excitation of single and coupled qubits for coherent quantum control and microwave detection

**Authors:** O. A. Ilinskaya, S. N. Shevchenko

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27610v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.27610v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-29


### 摘要

共振驱动能够对量子系统（包括单个和耦合量子位）进行一致控制。从补充的角度来看，量子系统的转变可以用于检测微波量子。在这项工作中，我们从理论上研究了量子位系统中的共振多子激发。当K个量子的能量与量子位系统的能量分裂相匹配时，这些量子的吸收会导致量子位的集体激发。我们重点关注两个耦合量子位的情况，并分析激发和相关过程的量子动力学。在只有一个量子位相关而其余量子位可以忽略的特定情况下，动力学允许进行分析处理。我们研究了多子共振、布洛赫-西格特位移和粒子数倒置，这些现象都是相干量子控制和微波量子检测的核心。


### Abstract

Resonant driving enables coherent control of quantum systems, including single and coupled qubits. From a complementary perspective, transitions of a quantum system can be exploited for the detection of microwave photons. In this work, we theoretically investigate resonant multiphoton excitations in a system of qubits. When the energy of K photons matches the energy splitting of the qubit system, the absorption of these photons leads to collective excitation of the qubits. We focus on the case of two coupled qubits and analyze the quantum dynamics of both excitation and relacation processes. In the particular case where only a single qubit is relevant and the remaining qubits can be neglected, the dynamics admits an analytical treatment. We examine multiphoton resonances, the Bloch-Siegert shift, and population inversion, phenomena that are central to both coherent quantum control and microwave photon detection.
