## 来自精确重置地图的相干控制量子芝诺动力学

**Original Title:** Coherence-Controlled Quantum Zeno Dynamics from Exact Reset Maps

**Authors:** Jishad Kumar, Achilleas Lazarides, Tapio Ala-Nissila

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27619v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.27619v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-29


### 摘要

我们为一类广泛的开放系统中的量子芝诺和反芝诺动力学开发了一个精确的框架，其微观Hamilton在玻色子或费米子操作员中是二次的。我们通过在单粒子密度矩阵（SDM）水平上起作用的精确频闪重置方案来处理环境。在这个框架内，我们考虑了两种情况：重复交互（RI）协议，其中环境块被重新加热并在每一步后擦除所有系统-环境相关性，以及进化相关（EC）协议，其中只有环境块被重置，而系统-环境相关性被保留。对于RI，我们推导出单粒子激发生存概率的一般短期芝诺定律，并表明相应的衰变率随重置间隔线性缩放，这意味着芝诺冻结在无限频繁重置的极限下。除了短期机制之外，我们直接根据精确的单周期传播子来公式化RI动态，这使我们能够在无需额外逼近的情况下分析有限的-$T $反芝诺窗口。对于EC，我们获得了连续重置描述，其中保留的单粒子相关器服从有限维线性方程。在这种情况下，系统块中的漂移在频率重置限制中保持有限，因此不存在严格的冻结。我们对单个费米子水平与充当结构化浴的半无限紧束缚链耦合来说明这些结果。我们的结果确定，相干擦除与相干保留是控制重置引发的Zeno物理学的关键因素。


### Abstract

We develop an exact framework for quantum Zeno and anti-Zeno dynamics in a broad class of open systems, whose microscopic Hamiltonians are quadratic in bosonic or fermionic operators. We treat the environment through an exact stroboscopic resetting scheme acting at the level of the single-particle density matrix (SPDM). Within this framework, we consider two cases: a repeated-interaction (RI) protocol, in which the environment block is rethermalized and all system-environment coherences are erased after each step, and an evolving-correlation (EC) protocol, in which only the environment block is reset while system-environment coherences are preserved. For RI, we derive a general short-time Zeno law for the survival probability of a single-particle excitation and show that the corresponding decay rate scales linearly with the reset interval, implying Zeno freezing in the limit of infinitely frequent resets. Beyond the short-time regime, we formulate the RI dynamics directly in terms of the exact one-cycle propagator, which allows us to analyze finite-$τ$ anti-Zeno windows without additional approximations. For EC, we obtain a continuous-reset description in which the kept single-particle correlators obey a finite-dimensional linear differential equation. In this case the drift in the system block remains finite in the frequent-reset limit, so strict freezing is absent. We illustrate these results for a single fermionic level coupled to a semi-infinite tight-binding chain acting as a structured bath. Our results identify coherence erasure versus coherence retention as the key factor controlling the reset-induced Zeno physics.


---


## $q$-变形量子力学和黑洞/白洞谱对的热力学

**Original Title:** $q$-Deformed Quantum Mechanics and the Thermodynamics of Black Hole/White Hole Spectral pair

**Authors:** S. Jalalzadeh, R. Jalalzadeh, H. Moradpour

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27621v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.27621v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-29


### 摘要

在这项工作中，我们研究了$q$-变形惠勒-德威特框架内史瓦西黑洞和白洞的热力学。通过在单位根处引入$q$-变形海森堡-Weyl代数，我们推导出有限维Hilbert空间、有界质量谱和导致有界质量关系的隔热不变量。变形会产生普遍的对数修正，以及与德西特界限相匹配的最低温度和最大的熵。此外，我们研究了冷残留物的解释，该冷残留物是动态稳定的，因为其辐射率接近零，尽管其热容量仍然为负。我们还探索了这种有限的信息量的全息含义。因此，我们的结果提供了一个一致的半经典图景，其中量子变形自然地引入了一个熵束缚，避免了最后蒸发阶段的分歧，并表明从量子引力到宇宙学的平稳过渡。


### Abstract

In this work, we investigate the thermodynamics of Schwarzschild black and white holes within a $q$-deformed Wheeler--DeWitt framework. By introducing a $q$-deformed Heisenberg--Weyl algebra at a root of unity, we derive a finite-dimensional Hilbert space, a bounded mass spectrum, and an adiabatic invariant leading to a bounded entropy-mass relation. The deformation results in a universal logarithmic correction, as well as a minimum temperature and a maximum entropy that matches the de Sitter bound. Also, we examine the interpretation of a cold remnant, which is dynamically stable because its radiation rate approaches zero, even though its heat capacity remains negative. We also explore the holographic implications of this limited entropy. Our results thus provide a consistent semiclassical picture, where quantum deformation naturally introduces an entropy bound, avoids divergences at the final evaporation stage, and suggests a smooth transition from quantum gravity to cosmology.


---


## 非均匀Dicke模型热化动力学的量子模拟

**Original Title:** Quantum simulation of thermalization dynamics of a nonuniform Dicke model

**Authors:** S. -A. Guo, J. Ye, J. -Y. Tan, Z. -W. Zhang, L. Zhang, Y. -Y. Chen, Y. -L. Xu, C. Zhang, Y. Jiang, B. -X. Qi, L. He, Z. -C. Zhou, Y. -K. Wu, L. -M. Duan

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27627v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.27627v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-29


### 摘要

以前在原子或离子系统中迪克模型的实验实现是基于假设均匀的旋转玻色子耦合的全局可观测量，而不可避免的实验非均匀性一方面需要对旋转状态进行现场分辨测量，另一方面提供了潜在的量子优势多旋转分布的模拟。在这里，我们报告了最多200个离子的二维（2D）晶体中的非均匀Dicke类模型的量子模拟。我们明确地证明了少旋转可观测量和多旋转分布对模型空间不均匀性的敏感性，并通过测量选定离子群的子系统熵来检查非均匀模型的热化动力学。我们的工作使得研究对称子空间之外的类迪克模型，为理解无序在其热化和量子混乱行为中的作用铺平了道路。


### Abstract

Previous experimental realizations of Dicke model in atomic or ionic systems are based on global observables assuming uniform spin-boson coupling, while inevitable experimental nonuniformity on the one hand requires site-resolved measurement of spin states, and on the other hand provides potential quantum advantage on the simulation of multi-spin distributions. Here we report the quantum simulation of a nonuniform Dicke-like model in a two-dimensional (2D) crystal of up to 200 ions. We explicitly demonstrate the sensitivity of few-spin observables and multi-spin distributions to the spatial inhomogeneity of the model, and examine the thermalization dynamics of the nonuniform model by measuring the subsystem entropies of selected ion groups. Our work enables the study of Dicke-like models beyond the symmetric subspace, paving the way toward understanding the role of disorder in its thermalization and quantum chaos behavior.

## 固定电路区域下量子神经网络中频谱和可训练性的编码族基准

**Original Title:** Benchmarking Encoding Families in Quantum Neural Networks Under Fixed Circuit Area for Frequency Spectrum and Trainability

**Authors:** Martyna Czuba, Patrick Holzer, Hein Zay Yar Oo

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27671v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.27671v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-29


### 摘要

量子神经网络（QNN）为将量子计算原理集成到机器学习中提供了一个有前途的框架，但其实际能力和局限性仍然没有得到充分的研究。在这项工作中，我们通过对合成和现实世界数据集的不同电路架构和编码策略进行基准测试，系统地研究QNN的可训练性和逼近性。我们分析了几个ansätze，包括Hamming、二进制、指数、三进制、turpike和Golomb，通过评估它们学习建模为随机有限傅里叶序列的合成数据的能力。为了评估现实世界的适用性，我们进一步评估了两个时间序列分类任务的QNN：Fischertechnik气动泄漏检测数据集和公开可用的NASA轴承故障数据集。我们的实验表明，虽然更宽的频谱在理论上可以提高表现力，但实际的可训练性受到量子位数和电路深度等架构因素的强烈影响。值得注意的是，我们发现，当频谱根据目标函数的复杂度定制时，QNN的性能最佳，但仍尽可能紧凑。此外，具有相同频谱的架构在可训练性方面可能不同，除了单层情况外，使用更多量子位和更少层的配置通常表现更好。这些发现为选择QNN ansätze提供了指导方针，并为量子机器学习中表达力和可训练性之间的相互作用提供了新的见解。


### Abstract

Quantum Neural Networks (QNNs) offer a promising framework for integrating quantum computing principles into machine learning, yet their practical capabilities and limitations remain insufficiently studied. In this work, we systematically investigate the trainability and approximation properties of QNNs by benchmarking diverse circuit architectures and encoding strategies across synthetic and real-world datasets. We analyze several ansätze, including Hamming, binary, exponential, ternary, turnpike and Golomb, by evaluating their ability to learn synthetic data modeled as random finite Fourier series. To assess real-world applicability, we further evaluate QNNs on two time-series classification tasks: a Fischertechnik pneumatic leak detection dataset and the publicly available NASA bearing fault dataset. Our experiments show that while broader frequency spectra can theoretically enhance expressivity, practical trainability is strongly influenced by architectural factors such as qubit count and circuit depth. Notably, we find that QNNs perform best when the frequency spectrum is tailored to the target function's complexity but remains as compact as possible. Moreover, architectures with identical frequency spectra can differ in trainability, with configurations using more qubits and fewer layers generally performing better, except in the single-layer case. These findings provide guidelines for selecting QNN ansätze and offer new insights into the interplay between expressivity and trainability in quantum machine learning.

## 交互式量子仪器的资源理论

**Original Title:** The resource theory of interactive quantum instruments

**Authors:** Chung-Yun Hsieh, Armin Tavakoli, Huan-Yu Ku, Paul Skrzypczyk

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27676v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.27676v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-29


### 摘要

量子仪器在测量过程中描述经典输出和更新的量子态。为了以非平凡的方式做到这一点，仪器必须能够与它们测量的状态进行一致的交互。在这里，我们开发了一个工具的资源理论。我们认为一个相关的量化器之间的分离互动和非互动的仪器，并表明，它承认三个不同的操作的量子信息任务的解释。这些涉及（i）局部测量后最大纠缠状态的保留，（ii）测量后保留随机状态的平均能力，以及（iii）恢复测量最大纠缠状态的一半产生的经典信息的能力。我们还引入了一组自然的允许操作，并表明第三个任务完全描述了仪器的资源内容。我们的一般框架复制了为渠道和测量建立的资源理论的特殊情况。


### Abstract

Quantum instruments describe both the classical output and the updated quantum state in a measurement process. To do this in a non-trivial way, instruments must have the capability to interact coherently with the state that they measure. Here, we develop a resource theory for instruments. We consider a relevant quantifier of the separation between interactive and non-interactive instruments and show that it admits three distinct operational interpretations in terms of quantum information tasks. These concern (i) the preservation of maximally entangled states after a local measurement, (ii) the average ability to preserve random states after measurement, and (iii) the ability to recover the classical information generated from measuring half of a maximally entangled state. We also introduce a natural set of allowed operations and show that the third task fully characterises the resource content of instruments. Our general framework reproduces as special cases established resource theories for channels and measurements.


---


## 引力子的腔QED传感器

**Original Title:** Cavity-QED Transducer of Gravitons

**Authors:** Fateme Shojaei Arani, Brahim Lamine, Jiro Soda

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27687v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.27687v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-29


### 摘要

我们开发了电磁波（EM）和引力波（GW）之间共振相互作用的量子描述。我们首先表明洛伦兹不变性和极化选择规则禁止自由空间中的任何光-引力子混合。我们证明，将EM场限制在腔量子电动力学（腔QED）环境内会打破平移对称性和各向同性，导致EM和重力自由度之间的非零模式耦合。在这个框架内，我们确定了多个光-引力子散射通道，包括量子上转换和下转换以及量子产生。在三线性相互作用的半经典极限中，GW充当经典泵，EM场处于真空中，自发参数量子放大和双模式压缩发生。然而，当引力场量子化时，与指数增长相反，量子和引力子之间的反作用和能量交换会导致放大饱和，并导致光子系统中纯度的损失。特征时间尺度为$t_{\text{p}}\sim（g\SQRT{n_g}）^{-1}$，其中$g$和$n_g$指的是耦合强度和平均引力子数，证明了与引力子占据数相互作用的集体增强。在受激区域中，最初填充了一个EM模，有效耦合进一步增强，类似于迪克型超辐射发射。这项工作介绍了一种基于腔的引力子传感器探测量子方面的GW。


### Abstract

We develop a quantum description of the resonant interaction between electromagnetic (EM) and gravitational waves (GW). We first show that Lorentz invariance together with polarization selection rules forbids any photon-graviton mixing in free space. We demonstrate that confining the EM field within a cavity quantum electrodynamics (cavity-QED) environment breaks translational symmetry and isotropy, leading to non-vanishing mode coupling between EM and gravitational degrees of freedom. Within this framework, we identify multiple photon-graviton scattering channels, including photon up- and down-conversion and photon creation. In the semiclassical limit of the trilinear interaction where GW acts as a classical pump and the EM field is in a vacuum, spontaneous parametric photon amplification and two-mode squeezing occur. When the gravitational field is quantized, however, the back-action and energy exchange between photons and gravitons result in saturation of amplification, in contrast to exponential growth, and the loss of purity in the photonic subsystem. The characteristic timescale scales as $t_{\text{sp}}\sim (g\sqrt{n_g})^{-1}$, where $g$ and $n_g$ refer to the coupling strength and the mean graviton number, demonstrating collective enhancement of the interaction with the graviton occupation number. In the stimulated regime, where one EM mode is initially populated, the effective coupling is further enhanced, analogous to Dicke-type superradiant emission. This work introduces a cavity-based graviton transducer for probing quantum aspects of GWs.


---


## 弯曲界面上表面等离子体激元的赫尔姆霍尔兹方程：用几何势控制协同性

**Original Title:** A Helmholtz Equation for Surface Plasmon Polaritons on Curved Interfaces: Controlling Cooperativity with Geometric Potentials

**Authors:** Florian Bönsel, Flore K. Kunst

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27702v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.27702v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-29


### 摘要

沿着弯曲的金属-介电界面传播的表面等离子体激元经历平坦表面上不存在的几何诱导的修饰。在这项工作中，我们推导出弱弯曲光滑界面上横向磁表面等离子体激元模式的协变有效二维波动方程。通过用具有自适应弯曲边界条件的麦克斯韦方程组微扰展开，我们找到了一个具有两个几何势项的赫尔姆霍尔兹方程，这些势项以一级进入外部弯曲：与外部弯曲成正比的各向同性贡献，以及产生自第二基本形式的无痕迹部分的各向异性操作员。这些线性弯曲势将凸界面和凹界面区分开来，与介电导体等对称约束系统中已知的二次势相反。我们表明我们的方程重现了球形和圆柱形界面的既定结果。我们进一步预测，当材料介电率之比等于黄金比例的平方时，各向异性贡献消失。作为一个应用，我们展示了通过表面等离子体相互作用的弯曲金属球体上的量子发射器环的与符号相关的合作频移以及弯曲驱动的超辐射和亚辐射衰变率的重新分布。


### Abstract

Surface plasmon polaritons propagating along curved metal-dielectric interfaces experience geometry-induced modifications absent on flat surfaces. In this work, we derive a covariant, effective two-dimensional wave equation for the transverse magnetic surface plasmon mode on weakly curved smooth interfaces. By perturbatively expanding Maxwell's equations with curvature-adapted boundary conditions, we find a Helmholtz equation with two geometric potential terms that enter at first order in the extrinsic curvature: an isotropic contribution proportional to the extrinsic curvature, and an anisotropic operator arising from the traceless part of the second fundamental form. These linear-in-curvature potentials distinguish convex from concave interfaces, in contrast to the quadratic potentials known from symmetrically confined systems such as dielectric waveguides. We show that our equation reproduces established results for spherical and cylindrical interfaces. We furthermore predict that the anisotropic contribution vanishes when the ratio of the material permittivities equals the square of the golden ratio. As an application, we demonstrate sign-dependent cooperative frequency shifts as well as a curvature-driven redistribution of superradiant and subradiant decay rates for a ring of quantum emitters on a curved metallic spheroid interacting through the surface plasmons.


---


## 俘获离子量子位中快速高保真纠缠门的光场数字预失真

**Original Title:** Digital Predistortion of Optical Fields for Fast and High-Fidelity Entangling Gates in Trapped-Ion Qubits

**Authors:** Jovan Markov, Yotam Shapira, Ayelet Hasson, Meir Alon, Avraham Gross, Nitzan Akerman, Roee Ozeri

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27761v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.27761v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-29


### 摘要

高保真量子门需要精确的经典控制信号，但传递这些信号的模拟硬件会引入非线性失真，从而降低门性能。我们演示了用于在基于$^{88}$Sr$^+$的捕获离子处理器中生成多音纠缠门波的声光调制器的数字预失真。通过测量和反相调制器的静态非线性幅度响应，我们应用一种前向修正，以扩展其线性工作范围并抑制寄生交调产物。门射束的光谱分析显示，主要的交调音调受到3- 5分贝的抑制，在估计的门误差阈值为10美元的情况下，可用的折射效率大约增加了一倍。直接的两量子位Bell状态保真度测量证实预失真能够持续提高纠缠门性能。校准并倒置方法是设备和平台不可知的，适用于量子处理器经典控制链中的任何非线性元件。


### Abstract

High-fidelity quantum gates require precise classical control signals, yet the analog hardware delivering these signals introduces nonlinear distortions that degrade gate performance. We demonstrate digital predistortion of an acousto-optic modulator used to generate multi-tone entangling-gate waveforms in a trapped-ion processor based on $^{88}$Sr$^+$. By measuring and inverting the static nonlinear amplitude response of the modulator, we apply a feed-forward correction that extends its linear operating range and suppresses spurious intermodulation products. Spectral analysis of the gate beam shows 3--5 dB suppression of the dominant intermodulation tones, approximately doubling the usable diffraction efficiency at a $10^{-3}$ estimated gate-error threshold. Direct two-qubit Bell-state fidelity measurements confirm that predistortion consistently improves entangling-gate performance. The calibrate-and-invert methodology is device and platform agnostic, applicable to any nonlinear element in the classical control chain of a quantum processor.

## 宇称编码旋转系统混合解码方案的基准模拟

**Original Title:** Benchmarking simulation of hybrid decoding scheme for parity-encoded spin systems

**Authors:** Yoshihiro Nambu

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27776v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.27776v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-29


### 摘要

本文介绍了一种适用于宇称编码旋转系统的实用混合解码方案的经典基准模拟，该方案非常适合开发基于片上超导技术的量子退热装置。我们比较了使用两种嵌入方案来模拟来自本地交互的全对全连接性来寻找最佳解决方案的性能：Sourlas、Lechner、Hauke和Zoller提出的SL ZZ模型，以及常用的次嵌入（ME）方案。我们发现，当与基于经典位翻转算法的读出后经典解码相结合时，SL ZZ方案比ME方案更高效，尽管SL ZZ方案本身的效率大大低于ME方案。


### Abstract

This paper presents classical benchmark simulations of a practical hybrid decoding scheme for parity-encoded spin systems, which is well-suited to the development of quantum annealing devices based on on-chip superconducting technology. We compared the performance of finding the optimal solution using two embedding schemes for emulating all-to-all connectivity from local interactions: the SLHZ model, proposed by Sourlas, Lechner, Hauke, and Zoller, and the commonly used minor embedding (ME) scheme. We found that the SLHZ scheme is more efficient than the ME scheme when combined with postreadout classical decoding based on the classical bit-flipping algorithm, although the SLHZ scheme itself is substantially less efficient than the ME scheme.

## 超越确定因果顺序的互补性

**Original Title:** Complementarity Beyond Definite Causal Order

**Authors:** Mohd Asad Siddiqui, Md Qutubuddin, Tabish Qureshi

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27780v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.27780v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-29


### 摘要

波粒二象性是量子力学的基石，传统上是在确定的因果顺序下表述的。我们研究当操作的时间顺序一致叠加时，互补性如何被修改，就像量子开关中一样。我们表明，不存在同时捕获路径互换性、空间一致性和因果顺序之间的一致性的通用线性加性互补关系。这揭示了空间资源和因果资源之间的根本分离，这些资源存在于不同的子系统上，因此不受单个量子状态的共同约束。虽然追踪有序量子位在简化量子检测器状态水平上恢复了标准的二元关系，但在简化描述的水平上无法访问因果顺序之间的一致性。为了捕捉这一贡献，我们引入了\{因果连贯性}，定义为顺序量子位的连贯性，它量化了替代因果顺序之间的干扰，并且在操作上是可测量的;我们构建了显式过程，其中空间二元性饱和，而因果连贯性最大。我们进一步表明，互补性承认基于因果自由度的不相容测量的状态相关的熵公式;与一般的状态相关关系不同，这种公式源于普适不确定性原理，并提供了典型的操作上有意义的描述。这些结果证明，互补性从根本上是由因果结构塑造的，通常不能仅在约化量子状态的水平上完全捕获。


### Abstract

Wave--particle duality is a cornerstone of quantum mechanics, traditionally formulated under definite causal order. We investigate how complementarity is modified when the temporal order of operations is coherently superposed, as in the quantum switch. We show that no universal linear additive complementarity relation exists that simultaneously captures path distinguishability, spatial coherence, and coherence between causal orders. This reveals a fundamental separation between spatial and causal resources, which reside on different subsystems and are therefore not jointly constrained by a single quantum state. While tracing out the order qubit recovers the standard duality relation at the level of the reduced quanton--detector state, coherence between causal orders is not accessible at the level of the reduced description. To capture this contribution, we introduce \emph{causal coherence}, defined as the coherence of the order qubit, which quantifies interference between alternative causal orders and is operationally measurable; we construct explicit processes in which spatial duality is saturated while causal coherence is maximal. We further show that complementarity admits a state-dependent entropic formulation based on incompatible measurements on the causal degree of freedom; unlike generic state-dependent relations, this formulation arises from a universal uncertainty principle and provides a canonical operationally meaningful description. These results establish that complementarity is fundamentally shaped by causal structure and cannot, in general, be fully captured at the level of reduced quantum states alone.


---


## 通过量子热处理双层kagome旋转冰中的层间电荷有序竞争和量子分子重组

**Original Title:** Competing interlayer charge order and quantum monopole reorganisation in bilayer kagome spin ice via quantum annealing

**Authors:** Kumar Ghosh

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27826v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.27826v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-29


### 摘要

受激磁铁中的磁单极是典型的细分准粒子，但没有实验平台同时调节它们的限制并保留冰规则物理学。在这里，我们利用D-Wave数据库2量子退火炉的原生双层架构来实现第一个可编程双平面kagome旋转冰，跨越$1{，}536$逻辑旋转，跨越$4\times13\times 14 $系统大小网格、层间耦合和量子驱动。我们发现，层间交换驱动了从铁电交错电荷有序到反铁电交错电荷有序的急剧转变，这是一种没有经典或单层类似物的Ice-II相，临界起点在$（J_{\perp}/J_1）'/J_1）''。将电荷结构因子限制为冰规则斑块揭示了比传统全斑块估计器的数量级增强，证明量子选择的电荷顺序对于缺陷稀释的探针来说是不可见的，并为未来的量子旋转冰实验建立了方法学标准。拉曼化学势的量子重正化为进入拉曼去量子区所需的跨激子电路-QED kagome冰设定了具体的工程目标。对于现有的Ni$_{81}$Fe$_{19}$纳米线双层架构，有三个可证伪的预测：临界层间分离、升高的拉曼激活温度以及已发布的X射线数据集中Ice-II信号的数量级增强，所有这些都可以在无需新制造的情况下进行测试。


### Abstract

Magnetic monopoles in frustrated magnets are paradigmatic fractionalised quasiparticles, yet no experimental platform simultaneously tunes their confinement and preserves ice-rule physics. Here we exploit the native bilayer architecture of a D-Wave Advantage2 quantum annealer to realise the first programmable two-plane kagome spin ice, spanning $1{,}536$ logical spins across a $4\times13\times14$ grid of system size, interlayer coupling, and quantum drive. We find that interlayer exchange drives a sharp transition from ferroelectric to antiferroelectric staggered charge order, an Ice-II phase with no classical or single-layer analogue, with a critical onset at $(J_{\perp}/J_1)^{*} \approx 0.044$ that is stable across five decades of annealing time. Restricting the charge structure factor to ice-rule plaquettes reveals an order-of-magnitude enhancement over conventional all-plaquette estimators, demonstrating that quantum-selected charge order is invisible to defect-diluted probes and establishing a methodological standard for future quantum spin ice experiments. The quantum renormalisation of the monopole chemical potential sets a concrete engineering target for the transmon circuit-QED kagome ice required to enter the monopole deconfinement regime. Three falsifiable predictions follow for existing Ni$_{81}$Fe$_{19}$ nanowire bilayer architectures: a critical interlayer separation, an elevated monopole activation temperature, and an order-of-magnitude enhancement of the Ice-II signal in published X-ray datasets, all testable without new fabrication.

## 极化子凝聚物中纯能量驰豫的研究

**Original Title:** Ground-State Selection by Pure Energy Relaxation in Polariton Condensates

**Authors:** D. A. Saltykova, A. V. Yulin, I. A. Shelykh

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27834v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.27834v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-29


### 摘要

我们研究了在纯能量松弛存在下通过激子库非相关泵送的消散激子-极化子凝聚物中的非平衡模式选择。对于在阈值处选择涡旋模式的受限系统，我们表明能量松弛定性地改变了凝结情景：随着泵的增加，渐进状态从涡旋凝结演变为旋转混合状态，然后演变为接地状态凝结。因此，纯能量松弛会破坏凝聚成激发态的稳定性，并促进了接地状态的选择。


### Abstract

We study nonequilibrium mode selection in dissipative exciton-polariton condensates incoherently pumped through an excitonic reservoir in the presence of pure energy relaxation. For a confined system in which a vortex mode is selected at threshold, we show that energy relaxation qualitatively changes the condensation scenario: as the pump increases, the asymptotic state evolves from a vortex condensate to a rotating mixed state and then to a ground-state condensate. Pure energy relaxation thus destabilizes condensation into excited states and promotes ground-state selection.

## Q-Bridge：通过LLM进行量子机器学习的代码翻译

**Original Title:** Q-Bridge: Code Translation for Quantum Machine Learning via LLMs

**Authors:** Runjia Zeng, Priyabrata Senapati, Ruixiang Tang, Dongfang Liu, Qiang Guan

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27836v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.27836v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-29


### 摘要

大型语言模型最近显示出弥合经典机器学习和量子机器学习之间差距的潜力。然而，缺乏标准化、高质量的数据集和强大的翻译框架限制了该领域的进展。我们引入Q-Bridge，这是一个LLM指导的代码翻译框架，可以系统地将CML实现转换为可执行的QML变体。我们的方法建立在一个自参与的管道之上，该管道将经过验证的种子代码库迭代地扩展到大规模数据集（CML-2-QML），集成可验证和不可验证的代码对。Q-Bridge模型使用监督式LoRA自适应进行微调，以实现可扩展和内存高效的训练，在不同架构中实现忠实且可解释的量子代码生成。实证分析证实了CML-QML直接翻译的可行性，并揭示了经典和量子范式之间一致的结构一致性。案例研究进一步证明，Q-Bridge可以保持确定性的正确性，并实现创造性的架构探索。这项工作为LLM驱动的量子代码翻译建立了第一个可重复的框架和数据集，为可扩展的量子人工智能开发提供了基础。


### Abstract

Large language models have recently shown potential in bridging the gap between classical machine learning and quantum machine learning. However, the lack of standardized, high-quality datasets and robust translation frameworks limits progress in this domain. We introduce Q-Bridge, an LLM-guided code translation framework that systematically converts CML implementations into executable QML variants. Our approach builds on a self-involving pipeline that iteratively expands a verified seed codebase into a large-scale dataset, CML-2-QML, integrating verifiable and unverifiable code pairs. The Q-Bridge model is fine-tuned using supervised LoRA adaptation for scalable and memory-efficient training, achieving faithful and interpretable quantum code generation across diverse architectures. Empirical analysis confirms the feasibility of direct CML-to-QML translation and reveals consistent structural alignment between classical and quantum paradigms. Case studies further demonstrate that Q-Bridge can maintain deterministic correctness and also enable creative architectural exploration. This work establishes the first reproducible framework and dataset for LLM-driven quantum code translation, offering a foundation for scalable quantum AI development.

## 用于多模式面部反欺骗的资源对齐混合量子经典框架

**Original Title:** A Resource-Aligned Hybrid Quantum-Classical Framework for Multimodal Face Anti-Spoofing

**Authors:** Wanqi Sun, Jungang Xu, Chenghua Duan

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27852v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.27852v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-29


### 摘要

将多维数据嵌入到资源有限的量子设备中仍然是实用量子机器学习的重大挑战。在多模式面部反欺骗中，虽然主成分分析等线性压缩方法可以降低维度以适应有限的量子预算，但此类方法通常会由于结构信息的丢失而失去关键的高级跨模式相关性。为此，我们提出了一种混合矩阵积状态（MPS）-变分量子电路（VQC）框架，其中MPS充当结构化、可区分的前量子压缩和融合模块，VQC充当量子分类器。该MPS模块建立在由虚拟键维控制的低阶结构之上，并与可配置的非线性增强机制集成，显式地建模远程跨模相关性，同时将多峰数据压缩为与量子预算相匹配的紧凑表示，并提高极端压缩下的数值稳定性。CASIA-SURF基准测试的实验表明，MPS-VQC在参数少于0.25 M的情况下实现了与强经典神经网络基线相当的准确性，凸显了在资源预算紧张的情况下，多维多峰数据的张量网络表示的参数效率。利用MPS结构和量子电路布局之间的固有兼容性，该框架不仅为NISQ设备上的高效多模式反欺骗提供了可行的技术途径，而且还作为未来全面量子实现此类任务的垫脚石。


### Abstract

Embedding high-dimensional data into resource-limited quantum devices remains a significant challenge for practical quantum machine learning. In multimodal face anti-spoofing, while linear compression methods such as principal component analysis can reduce dimensionality to accommodate limited quantum budgets, such approaches often lose critical high-order cross-modal correlations due to the loss of structural information. To this end, we propose a hybrid Matrix Product State (MPS)-Variational Quantum Circuit (VQC) framework, where the MPS serves as a structured, differentiable pre-quantum compression and fusion module, and the VQC acts as the quantum classifier. Built upon the low-rank structure controlled by the virtual bond dimension and integrated with a configurable nonlinear enhancement mechanism, this MPS module explicitly models long-range cross-modal correlations while compressing multimodal data into a compact representation matching the quantum budget and improving numerical stability under extreme compression. Experiments on the CASIA-SURF benchmark demonstrate that MPS-VQC achieves accuracy comparable to strong classical neural network baselines with fewer than 0.25M parameters, highlighting the parameter efficiency of tensor-network representations for high-dimensional multimodal data under tight resource budgets. Leveraging the intrinsic compatibility between MPS structures and quantum circuit topology, this framework not only provides a viable technological pathway for efficient multimodal anti-spoofing on NISQ devices but also serves as a stepping stone toward fully quantum implementations of such tasks in the future.

## 通过不受控制的个位数更便宜的一致相估计

**Original Title:** Exponentially cheaper coherent phase estimation via uncontrolled unitaries

**Authors:** Mirko Amico

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27858v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.27858v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-29


### 摘要

相反冲是许多量子算法（例如量子相估计）中使用的基本基元。在这里，我们观察到，通过使用有关受控单位的信息，我们可以用非受控单位替换受控单位，但代价是引入受控状态准备。然后，我们展示了当目标是估计其准备过程已知的本征态的相时，如何将这种修改后的相反冲用作量子相估计算法的一部分。我们证明，这会导致m位阶段估计的两量子位门数量在相关限制下呈指数级减少。还列出了应用程序的示例。当然，这可以适用于任何使用相反冲现象并满足假设的算法。


### Abstract

Phase kickback is a fundamental primitive that is used in many quantum algorithms, such as quantum phase estimation. Here we observe that by using information about the controlled unitary, we can replace the controlled unitary with an uncontrolled one at the cost of introducing controlled state preparations. We then show how this modified phase kickback can be used as part of the quantum phase estimation algorithm when the goal is to estimate the phase of an eigenstate whose preparation procedure is known. We prove that this yields an exponential reduction in the number of two-qubit gates for an m-bit phase estimation in the relevant limit. Examples of applications are also presented. Naturally, this can be adapted to any algorithm that uses the phase kickback phenomenon and satisfies the assumptions.

## 通过核旋转超极化增强光地址分子量子位的旋转相关性

**Original Title:** Enhancing Spin Coherence of Optically-Addressed Molecular Qubit by Nuclear Spin Hyperpolarization

**Authors:** Boning Li, Patrick Hautle, Duhan Zhang, Liangping Zhu, Paola Cappellaro, Tom Wenckebach, Yifan Quan

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27872v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.27872v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-29


### 摘要

光学可编址的分子三重态旋转为量子应用提供了一个化学可调的平台，但它们的一致性通常受到与周围旋转浴相互作用的限制。在这里，我们证明了对高纯度奈单晶体中共结晶的并五苯的光激发三重态旋转中核浴诱导的退散相关的受控抑制。通过通过三重动态核极化（三重DNP）超极化质子旋转浴，抑制了核旋转产生的磁噪音，导致电子旋转横向相干时间的延长。在实验上，我们观察到质子旋转浴的60%极化使旋转回声衰变时间增加了25%。所测量的旋转回声衰变时间（$T_2$）与核极化的比例定量遵循从极化控制的核二阶矩推导出的预测依赖性。通过簇相关扩展（CCE）模拟定量再现了相关时间的增强和绝对值。这些结果将核旋转超极化确立为一种通用且主动可调的方法来工程分子量子位的一致性。这项工作为高连贯性分子和固体旋转系统提供了一个广泛适用的设计框架。


### Abstract

Optically addressable molecular triplet spins provide a chemically tunable platform for quantum application, but their coherence is often limited by interactions with surrounding spin baths. Here we demonstrate controlled suppression of nuclear-bath-induced decoherence in photoexcited triplet spins of pentacene co-crystallized in high-purity naphthalene single crystals. By hyperpolarizing the proton spin bath through triplet dynamic nuclear polarization (triplet-DNP), magnetic noise generated by the nuclear spins is suppressed, leading to an extension of the electron spin transverse coherence time. Experimentally, we observe a 25\% enhancement of the spin-echo decay time with $60\%$ polarization of the proton spin bath. The measured scaling of the spin-echo decay time ($T_2$) with nuclear polarization quantitatively follows the predicted dependence derived from the polarization-controlled nuclear second moment. Both the enhancement and the absolute value of the coherence time are quantitatively reproduced by cluster correlation expansion (CCE) simulations. These results establish nuclear spin hyperpolarization as a general and actively tunable approach to engineering coherence in molecular qubits. This work provides a broadly applicable design framework for high-coherence molecular and solid-state spin systems.


---


## 基于几何最优控制理论的量子鲁棒控制

**Original Title:** Quantum Robust Control using Geometric Optimal Control Theory

**Authors:** Francesca Albertini, Domenico D'Alessandro

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27894v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.27894v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-29


### 摘要

在本文中，我们展示了一种基于几何最优控制工具的量子鲁棒控制方法。感兴趣的中心对象是灵敏度函数，其定义为轨迹相对于（未知、小）参数的泰勒展开中的系数，这些参数描述了实际模型与名义模型的偏差。根据这些量，我们形式化了一个最佳控制问题，其中搜索最佳名义轨迹，该轨迹最大限度地减少灵敏度的大小，同时考虑控制设计的其他方面，例如控制场的能量。   我们详细考虑了具有去相Hamilton项的单个量子比特的情况，以及通过最小化控制场能量和一阶灵敏度的加权和来获得状态转移的最优控制问题。在灵敏度上的权重非常大的限制下，我们获得最佳控制，使灵敏度归零并使控制场能量最小化。这个问题具有丰富的数学结构，可以用椭圆积分来解决它。对于这个问题，我们获得了一个显式解决方案，该解决方案特别简单且平滑，避免了其他方法中存在的不连续性。   我们将结果扩展到两个量子位的鲁棒控制，以最大限度地减少串话污染，因为我们表明这样的问题会分解为两个独立的一个量子位问题。


### Abstract

In this paper, we demonstrate an approach to quantum robust control based on the tools of geometric optimal control. The central objects of interest are the sensitivity functions defined as the coefficients in the Taylor expansion of the trajectory with respect to the (unknown, small) parameters which describe the deviation of the actual model from nominal one. In terms of these quantities, we formalize an optimal control problem where one searches for the optimal nominal trajectory which minimizes the size of the sensitivity while taking into account other aspects of the control design such as the energy of the control field.
  We consider in detail the case of a single qubit with a dephasing Hamiltonian term, and the optimal control problem of obtaining a state transfer by minimizing the weighted sum of the energy of the controlling field and the first order sensitivity. At the limit of a very large weight on the sensitivity, we obtain the optimal control which zeros the sensitivity and minimizes the control field energy. This problem has a rich mathematical structure which enables its solution in terms of elliptic integrals. For this problem, we obtain an explicit solution which is particularly simple and also smooth, avoiding discontinuities which are present in other approaches.
  We extend the results to the robust control of two quantum bits minimizing cross-talk contamination, as we show that such a problem decouples in two independent one qubit problems.

## 单个NV中心中的高PDMR对比度和相关的光电流特性

**Original Title:** High PDMR contrast in single NV centres and related photocurrent properties

**Authors:** Michael Petrov, Boo Carmans, Josef Soucek, Akhil Kuriakose, Ottavia Jedrkiewicz, Emilie Bourgeois, Milos Nesladek

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27911v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.27911v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-29


### 摘要

本文旨在加深对氮空位（NV）中心磁共振光电检测（PDMR）机制的理解。这项技术对于固态量子计算平台的开发尤其重要。特别是，我们报告了单个NV中心中光电流（PC）产生和电荷循环的新见解，这与PDMR对比度达到50%及以上有关。我们开发了一种定位PC相关功能的技术。我们发现，在NV中心产生的电子存储在接口陷阱水平，并建立接口状态作为一个放大器，可以通过引入第二激光到我们的共焦设置驱动。我们表明，控制这些界面状态可以显着提高PDMR对比度。我们开发了一个模型，始终解释观察到的放大效应，即使没有偏置电压的应用。


### Abstract

This paper aims to extend the understanding of the mechanism of photo-electrical detection of magnetic resonance (PDMR) in nitrogen-vacancy (NV) centres. This technique is particularly important for development of solid-state quantum computing platforms. In particular, we report on the new insight in the photocurrent (PC) generation and charge cycling in the single NV centre, which is related to PDMR contrast reaching 50\% and above. We develop a technique to locate PC related features. We find that electrons generated at the NV centre are stored in interface trap levels and establish that the interface states serve as an amplifier that can be driven by introducing a second laser into our confocal setup. We show that controlling these interface states allows one to significantly enhance the PDMR contrast. We develop a model that consistently explains observed amplification effects even without the application of a bias voltage.

## 基于态鉴别的量子非破坏测量的上下文性

**Original Title:** Contextuality of quantum non-demolition measurement via state discrimination

**Authors:** Min Namkung, Ilhwan Kim, Hyang-Tag Lim

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27917v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.27917v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-30


### 摘要

量子非破坏测量促进了各种量子技术，包括量子通信。值得注意的是，它们的操作结构可以通过经典模型（称为非上下文模型）复制，这使得识别哪些特征阻止此类模型再现相应的量子测量变得至关重要。在这项工作中，我们从理论上证明了量子非破坏测量结构中固有的上下文特征。这些特征不仅揭示了无二义性态鉴别的非经典性，而且还扩展到序列无二义性鉴别和概率量子克隆，这两者都涉及后测量态。此外，我们的分析扩展到有噪音的场景，强调了其与实际实施的潜在相关性。我们相信，我们的结果拓宽了观察量子系统中非经典性的范围，并最终有助于各种量子技术的进步。


### Abstract

Quantum non-demolition measurements facilitate various quantum technologies, including quantum communication. Notably, their operational structure can be replicated by a classical model--referred to as a noncontextual model--making it crucial to identify which features prevents such models from reproducing the corresponding quantum measurements. In this work, we theoretically demonstrate contextual features inherent in the structure of quantum non-demolition measurements. These features not only reveal the nonclassicality of unambiguous state discrimination, but also extend to sequential unambiguous discrimination and probabilistic quantum cloning, both of which involve post-measurement states. Moreover, our analysis extends to noisy scenarios, highlighting its potential relevance for practical implementations. We believe that our results broaden the scope of observing nonclassicality in quantum systems and ultimately contribute to the advancement of various quantum technologies.

## 可靠激励状态变分量子紧缩的混合QPE-模拟策略

**Original Title:** Hybrid QPE-Ansatz Strategy for Reliable Excited-State Variational Quantum Deflation

**Authors:** Young Kyun Ahn, Young Min Rhee

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27978v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.27978v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-30


### 摘要

我们引入了一个保持对称性的旋转$z$-分量（$S_{z}$）和一个旋转$x$（$S_x$）的浅层量子相估计（QPE）例程，并将它们组合成一个用于有噪音的中尺度量子（NISQ）计算时代激发态计算的旋转过滤变分量子压缩（sfVQD）方案。该方案通过在$\mathrm{BEP}（i °\hat{S}_{x}）$下的受控旋转将旋转信息编码到一个小型辅助寄存器中，仅需适度的电路负载。然后，利用编码信息通过筛选来抑制旋转污染，避免对总旋转$\langle\hat{S}\rangle$进行昂贵的显式评估。由于筛选模块独立于变分方程运行，因此它还可以与基于变分量子本征解器的其他激发态计算方案一起使用。作为一个演示，我们将sfVQD应用于具有不同几何形状的LiH和BeH$_2$，以显示与没有QPE衍生筛选的传统VQD相比，单重态和三重态流管的分离显着改善。这些结果表明，辅助对称性筛选提供了一种模块化和NISQ兼容的途径来确保物理有意义的性质的激发态计算。我们讨论如何将我们的方案自然地扩展到计算其他保守量。


### Abstract

We introduce a spin $z$-component ($S_{z}$) conserving symmetry-preserving ansatz and a shallow quantum phase estimation (QPE) routine of spin $x$ ($S_x$), and combine them into a spin-filtering variational quantum deflation (sfVQD) scheme for noisy intermediate-scale quantum (NISQ) computing era excited state calculations. The scheme encodes the spin information into a small ancilla register through controlled rotations under $\mathrm{exp} (iθ\hat{S}_{x})$ with only modest circuit overhead. The encoded information is then utilized to suppress spin contamination by screening, avoiding costly explicit evaluation on the total spin $\langle\hat{S}^{2}\rangle$. Because the screening module operates independently of the variational ansatz, it can also be employed with other excited-state calculation schemes based on variational quantum eigensolvers. As a demonstration, we apply sfVQD to LiH and BeH$_2$ with varying geometries to show markedly improved separation of singlet and triplet manifolds over conventional VQD without QPE-derived screening. These results suggest that ancilla-assisted symmetry screening provides a modular and NISQ-compatible route to securing excited state calculations of physically meaningful properties. We discuss how our scheme may naturally be extended to computing other conserved quantities.

## 高效光催化产氢和有机污染降解的石墨-C3 N4/TiO 2（B）S-方案异结

**Original Title:** Graphitic-C3N4/TiO2(B) S-scheme Heterojunctions for Efficient Photocatalytic H2 Production and Organic Pollution Degradation

**Authors:** Xiaoyi Zhou, Min Zhang, Qiushi Wang, Shiwen Du, Xuedong Jing, Zhenyi Zhang

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.27989v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.27989v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-30


### 摘要

实现宽的太阳光谱吸收和强的氧化还原能力对于半导体光催化剂在环境修复和能源转化中至关重要。在此，通过将TiO2（B）纳米棒与g-C3 N4纳米片偶联来构建S-方案异结光催化剂。其匹配良好的能带结构将光吸收从紫外线扩展到可见光区域，并实现有效的电荷分离。在模拟阳光照射下，40wt%g-C3 N4/TiO2（B）异结在以甲醇为牺牲剂的水还原中提供了1.98 mmolg-1 h-1的H2释放速率，分别比纯g-C3 N4和TiO2（B）高1.5倍和2.0倍。当暴露于阿莫西林废水而不是甲醇溶液时，该异结在90分钟内降解了98.2%的阿莫西林，并产生20.70 umol g-1的H2。此外，由于S-方案电荷分离机制，该异结对各种有机抗生素和染料表现出优异的光降解活性。这项工作强调了S-方案异结在光催化氢气生产与有机废水处理方面的广阔潜力。


### Abstract

Achieving both broad solar-spectrum absorption and strong redox capability is critical for semiconductor photocatalysts in environmental remediation and energy conversion. Herein, an S-scheme heterojunction photocatalyst is constructed by coupling TiO2(B) nanorods with g-C3N4 nanosheets. Its well-matched band structure extends light absorption from the UV to the visible region and enables efficient charge separation. Under simulated sunlight irradiation, the 40 wt% g-C3N4/TiO2(B) heterojunction delivers a H2 evolution rate of 1.98 mmol g-1 h-1 for water reduction with methanol as the sacrificial agent, which is 1.5 and 2.0 times higher than those of pure g-C3N4 and TiO2(B), respectively. When exposed to amoxicillin wastewater instead of methanol solution, the heterojunction degrades 98.2% of amoxicillin and produces 20.70 umol g-1 of H2 within 90 min. Moreover, the heterojunction shows excellent photodegradation activity toward various organic antibiotics and dyes, owing to the S-scheme charge separation mechanism. This work highlights the promising potential of S-scheme heterojunctions for photocatalytic H2 production coupled with organic wastewater treatment.

## 具有延时相干反馈的人工原子的共振荧光

**Original Title:** Resonance fluorescence of an artificial atom with a time-delayed coherent feedback

**Authors:** Ching-Yeh Chen, Gavin Crowder, Zheng-Qi Niu, Ping Yi Wen, Yen-Hsiang Lin, Jeng-Chung Chen, Zhi-Rong Lin, Franco Nori, Stephen Hughes, Io-Chun Hoi

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28004v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.28004v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-30


### 摘要

量子电动力学中的光物质相互作用模型通常依赖于马尔科夫逼近，该逼近假设系统的未来演变仅取决于其当前状态，有效地将其视为一个“无记忆”过程。然而，这种近似在延迟效应显着的情况下无效。这些记忆和延迟效应有潜力改进现有的量子技术（例如，大规模量子网络、量子信息处理）并为未来应用解锁新现象。在这项工作中，我们展示了在线性和非线性激发状态下使用嵌入在超导体电路导体中的转子人工原子（视为量子位）的延时相干反馈系统的理论和实验。通过使用延迟时间与量子位松弛时间相当的反馈环，量子位进化的动态中出现了明显的非马尔科夫效应。我们还展示了如何通过量子位和反馈环之间的相互作用显着修改共振荧光光谱，包括弹性和非弹性散射（例如众所周知的Mollow三重组），以显示真正的非马尔科夫和量子非线性现象，这些现象无法用瞬时耦合参数来解释。这项工作提出了非马尔科夫政权中Mollow三胞胎的第一份实验报告。


### Abstract

The model of light-matter interaction in quantum electrodynamics typically relies on the Markovian approximation, which assumes that the system's future evolution depends solely on its current state, effectively treating it as a ``memoryless" process. However, this approximation is not valid in scenarios when retardation effects are significant. These memory and retardation effects have the potential to improve existing quantum technologies (e.g., large-scale quantum networks, quantum information processing) and unlock new phenomena for future applications. In this work, we show theory and experiments of a time-delayed coherent feedback system using a transmon artificial atom (treated as a qubit) embedded in a superconducting circuit waveguide, in both linear and nonlinear excitation regimes. By using a feedback loop with a delay time comparable to the qubit relaxation time, pronounced non-Markovian effects appear in the dynamics of the qubit evolution. We also show how the resonance fluorescence spectrum, including elastic and inelastic scattering (such as the well-known Mollow triplet), can be significantly modified through the interaction between the qubit and feedback loop to show genuine non-Markovian and quantum nonlinear phenomena that cannot be explained with instantaneous coupling parameters. This work presents the first experimental report of Mollow triplets in the non-Markovian regime.


---


## 移动镜子中的自我反思

**Original Title:** Self-Reflection in a Moving Mirror

**Authors:** Michael R. R. Good, Eric V. Linder

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28030v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.28030v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-30


### 摘要

我们提出了霍金型发射的分析平时空加速边界模拟，它具有无限的渐进加速度（以及黑洞模拟中的辐射速度），但总辐射能有限（以及黑洞模拟中的零表面重力）。我们在单个封闭模型内对其散射对称性、视界形成、渐进极端加速度、有限总辐射能量以及局部能流和全球粒子产生之间的区别进行了统一研究。推导出粒子谱、能谱和等效时空度量，揭示了正常和极端黑洞性质的有趣混合。


### Abstract

We present an analytic flat-spacetime accelerating boundary analog of Hawking-type emission that possesses infinite asymptotic acceleration (and radial acceleration in the black hole analog) but finite total radiated energy (and zero surface gravity in the black hole analog). We perform a unified study of its scattering symmetry, horizon formation, asymptotically extreme acceleration, finite total radiated energy, and the distinction between local energy flux and global particle production within a single closed-form model. The particle spectrum, energy spectrum, and equivalent spacetime metric are derived, revealing an interesting mix of normal and extremal black hole properties.

## 量子增强马尔科夫链的隔热修饰

**Original Title:** Adiabatic dressing of quantum enhanced Markov chains

**Authors:** Wen Ting Hsieh, Alev Orfi, Dries Sels

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28076v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.28076v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-30


### 摘要

量子增强马尔科夫链蒙特卡洛是一种混合量子经典算法，其中配置由量子提议者提出，并由经典算法接受或拒绝，已被引入作为鲁棒量子加速的可能方法。之前的工作已经确定了限制算法性能的竞争因素：量子动力学应该在一系列经典状态中对系统进行离域，以提出超出简单经典更新范围的配置，而过度的离域会产生不太可能被接受的配置，从而减慢链的收敛。在这里，我们表明，通过对激冷协议进行热力修饰来控制离域程度可以显着增强范式旋转玻璃模型中的马尔科夫间隙。


### Abstract

Quantum-enhanced Markov chain Monte Carlo, a hybrid quantum-classical algorithm in which configurations are proposed by a quantum proposer and accepted or rejected by a classical algorithm, has been introduced as a possible method for robust quantum speedup. Previous work has identified competing factors that limit the algorithm's performance: the quantum dynamics should delocalize the system across a range of classical states to propose configurations beyond the reach of simple classical updates, whereas excessive delocalization produces configurations unlikely to be accepted, slowing the chain's convergence. Here, we show that controlling the degree of delocalization by adiabatically dressing the quench protocol can significantly enhance the Markov gap in paradigmatic spin-glass models.

## 任意压缩Fock态的纠缠产生

**Original Title:** Entanglement generation of arbitrary squeezed Fock states

**Authors:** Qin-Ru Cheng, Ke-Xiong Yan, Yuan Qiu, Yi-Tong Shi, Yan Xia, Ye-Hong Chen

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28077v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.28077v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-30


### 摘要

我们提出了一种高效且鲁棒的协议，用于在高温量子位和压缩腔之间产生纠缠。通过对与量子位耦合的腔体应用参数驱动，系统的动态演变由压缩参考系内的各向异性拉比模型精确描述。利用高级时间平均方法，我们解析地推导出了高级三量子过程的共振条件和有效拉比频率。通过实施隔热通道，缓慢调节整个共振的腔频率，系统被引导到最大纠缠状态，例如，在压缩图像中的三光子态$\ket{g，3}$和量子比特激发态$\ket{e，0}$之间。数值仿真结果证实了所提出的协议的高保真度和鲁棒性。我们的方法为产生复杂的非高斯纠缠态提供了一条实用的途径，这些纠缠态对于超出标准量子极限的容错量子计算和量子计量学具有重要价值。


### Abstract

We propose an efficient and robust protocol for the generation of entanglement between a superconducting qubit and a squeezed cavity. By applying a parametric drive to the cavity coupled to the qubit, the dynamical evolution of the system is precisely described by an anisotropic Rabi model within a squeezed reference frame. Utilizing high-order time-averaging methods, we analytically derive the resonance conditions and the effective Rabi frequency for the high-order three-photon process. By implementing an adiabatic passage, slowly tuning the cavity frequency across the resonance, the system is steered into a maximally entangled state, e.g., between the three-photon state $\ket{g,3}$ and the qubit excited state $\ket{e,0}$ in the squeezed picture. Numerical simulation results confirm the high fidelity and robustness of the proposed protocol. Our method provides a practical pathway for generating complex non-Gaussian entangled states, which are of significant value for fault-tolerant quantum computation and quantum metrology beyond the standard quantum limit.

## 具有稳健自我测试的设备独立量子密钥分发

**Original Title:** Device independent quantum key distribution with robust self-tests

**Authors:** Andreas Bluhm, Gereon Koßmann, René Schwonnek

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28085v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.28085v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-30


### 摘要

与设备无关的量子密钥分发（DIQKD）提供了一种具有最少假设和高度抽象的理论构建模块的量子密钥分发模型。尽管DIQKD使我们摆脱了对特定设备模型和相关误差参数的详细讨论，但它用有关量子实验有效性的基本假设取代了它们。在这项工作中，我们提出了一种方法，通过在两个密钥生成方的实验室中执行本地自我测试，将基于DIQKD风格假设的协议提升为依赖设备的QKD协议。特别是，我们将路由Bell测试设置视为认真自我测试本地各方的一种手段，并开发了一个严格的数学框架，表明潜在的优化问题确实可以转移到与设备相关的QKD设置。作为一个应用程序，我们通过路由BB 84协议的案例研究来说明许多相关技术。


### Abstract

Device-independent quantum key distribution (DIQKD) provides a model of quantum key distribution with minimal assumptions and highly abstract theoretical building blocks. Although DIQKD frees us from detailed discussions of specific device models and associated error parameters, it replaces them with fundamental assumptions about the validity of quantum experiments. In this work, we propose a way to lift a protocol based on DIQKD-style assumptions to a device-dependent QKD protocol by performing local self-tests in the laboratories of the two key-generating parties. In particular, we consider routed Bell-test setups as a means of self-testing the local parties in earnest and develop a rigorous mathematical framework showing that the underlying optimization problems can indeed be transferred to the device-dependent QKD setting. As an application, we illustrate many of the relevant techniques through the case study of a routed BB84 protocol.

## Q-DIPER：利用脑电数据进行集成量子转移学习和可区分量子架构搜索

**Original Title:** Q-DIVER: Integrated Quantum Transfer Learning and Differentiable Quantum Architecture Search with EEG Data

**Authors:** Junghoon Justin Park, Yeonghyeon Park, Jiook Cha

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28122v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.28122v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-30


### 摘要

由于启发式设计限制，将量子电路集成到深度学习管道中仍然具有挑战性。我们提出了Q-DIPER，这是一个混合框架，将大规模预训练的脑电编码器（DIPER-1）与可微量子分类器相结合。与固定模拟方法不同，我们采用可区分量子架构搜索来在端到端微调期间自主发现任务最优的电路布局。在PhysoNet Motor Imagery数据集上，我们的量子分类器实现了与经典多层感知器相当的预测性能（测试F1：63.49\%），同时使用大约\textBF{50 $\times $更少的任务特定头部参数}（2.10M vs. 105.02M）。这些结果验证了量子迁移学习作为一种参数有效的策略，用于高维生物信号处理。


### Abstract

Integrating quantum circuits into deep learning pipelines remains challenging due to heuristic design limitations. We propose Q-DIVER, a hybrid framework combining a large-scale pretrained EEG encoder (DIVER-1) with a differentiable quantum classifier. Unlike fixed-ansatz approaches, we employ Differentiable Quantum Architecture Search to autonomously discover task-optimal circuit topologies during end-to-end fine-tuning. On the PhysioNet Motor Imagery dataset, our quantum classifier achieves predictive performance comparable to classical multi-layer perceptrons (Test F1: 63.49\%) while using approximately \textbf{50$\times$ fewer task-specific head parameters} (2.10M vs. 105.02M). These results validate quantum transfer learning as a parameter-efficient strategy for high-dimensional biological signal processing.

## 可编程偶极旋转冰的量子相关区

**Original Title:** Quantum-Coherent Regime of Programmable Dipolar Spin Ice

**Authors:** Krzysztof Giergiel, Piotr Surówka

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28125v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.28125v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-30


### 摘要

受挫的旋冰系统支持新兴规范场和充当磁单极的分裂准粒子。尽管人工平台已经实现了直接可视化，但对其量子一致动力学的访问仍然有限。在这里，我们使用导电量子位量子退火炉实现了一个可编程的偶极方形旋转冰模型，从而提供了对之前未探索的人工旋转冰的量子相干区域的访问。通过实现格子旋转和物理量子位之间的直接一对一映射，结合工程扩展耦合，我们在包含400多个顶点的受挫折格子上实现了有效的偶极相互作用。调节横向场涨落使我们能够探索狄拉克弦缺陷和相互作用的拉曼等离子体的实时动态。我们观察到超扩散拉曼传输，标度指数介于经典扩散和弹道运动之间，表明超越经典随机松弛的动力学，并与涌现规范管内的连贯传播一致。这些结果将可编程量子旋转冰建立为研究工程量子物质中的细分激发和新兴规范动力学的可扩展平台。


### Abstract

Frustrated spin-ice systems support emergent gauge fields and fractionalized quasiparticles that act as magnetic monopoles. Although artificial platforms have enabled their direct visualization, access to their quantum-coherent dynamics has remained limited. Here we realize a programmable dipolar square spin-ice model using a superconducting-qubit quantum annealer, providing access to a previously unexplored quantum-coherent regime of artificial spin ice. By implementing a direct one-to-one mapping between lattice spins and physical qubits, together with engineered extended couplings, we realize effective dipolar interactions on frustrated lattices comprising more than 400 vertices. Tuning transverse-field fluctuations enables us to probe the real-time dynamics of Dirac-string defects and interacting monopole plasmas. We observe super-diffusive monopole transport, with scaling exponents intermediate between classical diffusion and ballistic motion, indicating dynamics beyond classical stochastic relaxation and consistent with coherent propagation within an emergent gauge manifold. These results establish programmable quantum spin ice as a scalable platform for investigating fractionalized excitations and emergent gauge dynamics in engineered quantum matter.

## 通过非厄米特格子中的虚规范相印记实现精确的皮肤临界相和可配置的分数波函数

**Original Title:** Exact Skin Critical Phase and Configurable Fractal Wavefunctions via Imaginary Gauge Phase Imprint in Non-Hermitian Lattices

**Authors:** Ji-Long Dong, Shi-Liang Zhu, Dan-Wei Zhang

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28153v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.28153v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-30


### 摘要

多重分数形临界状态等复杂状态的产生一直是经典和量子物理学中的一个突出挑战。在这里，我们提出了一个一般框架，称为虚规范相印记，允许在任何维非厄米特格子中设计严格的波函数。使用这种方法，我们发现了一个具有一维（和二维）精确临界波函数的新阶段，称为皮肤临界阶段（SCP）。与具有总体均匀密度分布和非埃尔米特集肤效应且在开放边界处具有本征状态积累的传统临界相不同，SCP的特征是宏观多重分数形分布，所有临界本征状态共享相同的轮廓，并且总是在周期性边界条件下在特定的体界面处积累，这成为开放边界条件下的与拓扑相关的边界或界面集肤模式。我们还展示了SCP中的弹道动力学，与传统关键阶段的扩散行为形成鲜明对比。此外，我们通过在更高维度上压印可配置波函数来验证我们的方法，包括非分数格中具有谢尔宾斯基地毯和科赫雪花轮廓的复杂分数形状态以及非莫尔格中的莫尔状态。我们的工作不仅为分数形现象和关键阶段提供了新的见解，而且为工程非埃尔米特系统中的波操纵提供了严格的范式。


### Abstract

The generation of complex states like multifractal critical states has been an outstanding challenge in both classical and quantum physics. Here we propose a general framework, termed the imaginary gauge phase imprint, allowing to engineer rigorous wavefunctions in any-dimensional non-Hermitian lattices. Using this method, we uncover a novel phase with exact critical wavefunctions in one (and two) dimension, dubbed the skin critical phase (SCP). Unlike conventional critical phases with overall uniform density distributions and non-Hermitian skin effect with eigenstate accumulation at open boundaries, the SCP is marked by a macroscopically multifractal distribution with all critical eigenstates sharing an identical profile and always accumulating at specific bulk interfaces under periodic boundary condition, which become topology-dependent boundary or interface skin modes under open boundary condition. We also show the ballistic dynamics in the SCP, in contrast to the diffusive behaviour in conventional critical phases. Moreover, we validate our method by imprinting configurable wavefunctions in higher dimensions, including complex fractal states with Sierpinski-carpet and Koch-snowflake profiles in non-fractal lattices and Moire states in non-Moire lattices. Our work not only offers fresh insights into fractal phenomena and critical phases, but also provides a rigorous paradigm for wave manipulations in engineered non-Hermitian systems.


---


## 精确的$\mathbb{Z}_2$\mathbb{Z}_2 $复律码非Clifford

**Original Title:** Exact $\mathbb{Z}_2$ electromagnetic duality of $\mathbb{Z}_2$ toric code is non-Clifford

**Authors:** Ryohei Kobayashi

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28230v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.28230v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-30


### 摘要

2D $\mathbb{Z}_2$复律码承认交换电和磁准粒子的全球对称性，称为电磁二元论。已知的实现包括格子平移对称性、由Clifford电路生成的精确$\mathbb{Z}_4$对称性以及由非Clifford电路生成的精确$\mathbb{Z}_2$对称性。我们表明克利福德电磁二元性无法实现精确的内部$\mathbb{Z}_2$对称性。对于通用奇$l$，对于具有粗翻译不变性的对称性，这一点通过$l$格单位得到了严格证明。因此，精确的内部$\mathbb{Z}_2$电磁二元性必须是非Clifford的，而一般的内部Clifford实现必然具有$\mathbb{Z}_{2#m}$代数，其中$m\ge 2$。我们的结果表明精确的电磁二元性和克利福德电路层次之间存在意想不到的联系。


### Abstract

The 2D $\mathbb{Z}_2$ toric code admits a global symmetry exchanging electric and magnetic quasiparticles, known as electromagnetic duality. Known realizations include lattice translation symmetry, an exact $\mathbb{Z}_4$ symmetry generated by a Clifford circuit, and an exact $\mathbb{Z}_2$ symmetry generated by a non-Clifford circuit. We show that a Clifford electromagnetic duality cannot realize an exact internal $\mathbb{Z}_2$ symmetry. This is proved rigorously for symmetries with coarse translation invariance by $l$ lattice units for generic odd $l$. Therefore an exact internal $\mathbb{Z}_2$ electromagnetic duality must be non-Clifford, whereas generic internal Clifford realization necessarily has $\mathbb{Z}_{2^m}$ algebra with $m\ge 2$. Our result suggests an unexpected connection between exact electromagnetic duality and Clifford hierarchy of circuits.


---


## 利用陷阱诱导共振的超冷极性分子量子工程

**Original Title:** Quantum engineering with ultracold polar molecules using trap-induced resonances

**Authors:** Sakthikumaran Ravichandran, Piotr Kulik, Krzysztof Jachymski

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28270v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.28270v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-30


### 摘要

极地分子代表了量子模拟和计算协议的一个有前途的平台。高度可控的光镊子阵列现在可以在实验中使用，从而可以对单个分子进行前所未有的控制。运动移相通常被视为量子计算场景中的障碍。在这里，我们考虑使用陷阱结构作为实现高效量子门的资源。通过数值求解被困在单独镊子中的偶极的二体问题，我们确定了陷阱诱导的共振，它可以作为实现状态相关动力学的机制，并可以进一步用于量子传感。


### Abstract

Polar molecules represent a promising platform for quantum simulation and computation protocols. Highly controllable arrays of optical tweezers are now accessible in experiments, allowing for unprecedented control of individual molecules. Motional dephasing is typically seen as an obstacle in quantum computing scenarios. Here, we instead consider using the trap structure as a resource for implementing efficient quantum gates. By numerically solving the two-body problem of dipoles trapped in separate tweezers, we identify trap-induced resonances that can serve as the mechanism for achieving state-dependent dynamics and can be further utilized for quantum sensing.

## 真实和非真实量子非市场性：统一的信息理论评论

**Original Title:** Genuine and Non-Genuine Quantum Non-Marketability: A Unified Information-Theoretic Review

**Authors:** Rajeev Gangwar, Ujjwal Sen

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28277v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.28277v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-30


### 摘要

了解开放量子动力学的特征是否真正量子仍然是量子动力学的核心挑战。尽管量子动力学的非马尔科夫行为已在不同环境中得到广泛研究，但对于动力学的哪些性质反映了真正的量子特征，哪些性质源自经典或非真正的量子来源，仍然没有达成共识。在这篇评论中，我们提供了基于信息回流及其起源性质来描述量子非马尔科夫性的最新进展的详细信息。我们还对各种方法如何区分经典和量子贡献，以及它们如何定义揭示真正量子非马尔科夫性的操作任务进行了调查。我们分析了几个框架，包括基于状态可分配性、基于通道（“CP可分割性”）和过程张量方法。对于每个框架，我们概述了潜在的物理动机，即为区分真正的量子非马尔科夫性与实际或明显的记忆效应而提出的标准。我们进一步比较不同的方法及其优点和局限性。该评论旨在根据量子非马尔科夫过程的性质澄清量子非马尔科夫过程的概念和操作方面，并为未来对量子非马尔科夫过程及其在推进量子信息科学和技术中的作用的研究提供基础。


### Abstract

Understanding whether the features of open quantum dynamics are genuinely quantum remains a central challenge in quantum dynamics. Even though the non-Markovian behavior of quantum dynamics has been widely investigated across different settings, there is still no consensus on which properties of a dynamics reflect genuine quantum features and which arise from classical or non-genuine quantum sources. In this review, we provide detailed information on recent developments in characterizing quantum non-Markovianity based on information backflow and the nature of its origin. We also present a survey on how various approaches separate classical and quantum contributions, as well as how they define operational tasks that reveal genuine quantum non-Markovianity. We analyze several frameworks, including state-distinguishability -based, channel-based (``CP-divisibility''), and process-tensor methods. For each framework, we outline the underlying physical motivation, the criteria proposed to distinguish genuine quantum non-Markovianity from practical or apparent memory effects. We further compare different approaches and their strengths and limitations. The review aims to clarify the conceptual and operational aspects of quantum non-Markovian processes based on their nature and to provide a foundation for future research on quantum non-Markovianity and its role in advancing quantum information science and technology.


---


## 最低维度的纠缠与一类地方国家歧视问题

**Original Title:** Entanglement of minimal dimension and a class of local state discrimination problems

**Authors:** Saronath Halder, Suchetana Goswami

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28284v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.28284v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-30


### 摘要

在这项工作中，我们构建了一小群二分垂直纯状态，这些状态无法通过局部操作和经典通信（LOCC）完美区分。我们提到，并非构造集中的所有状态都一定是纠缠的。然而，这样的集合至少包含一个纠缠态，该纠缠态无法被LOCC（非零概率）最终识别。然后，我们证明，任何此类集合的状态都可以通过LOCC使用最小维纠缠资源状态来完美区分。显然，在这里，纠缠资源状态提供了优势，而与给定集合的维度无关。利用这一结果，我们还证明了任何纯纠缠态都可以作为在LOCC下以非零概率明确区分任何当前集合的状态的资源。这些集合存在于所有二进制的希尔伯特空间中。此外，可以减少这样一个集合的平均纠缠含量或增加集合的基数，而不改变集合的某些性质。


### Abstract

In this work, we construct small sets of bipartite orthogonal pure states that cannot be perfectly distinguished by local operations and classical communication (LOCC). We mention that not all the states within the constructed sets are necessarily entangled. However, such a set contains at least one entangled state which cannot be conclusively identified by LOCC (with nonzero probability). Then, we show that the states of any such set can be perfectly distinguished by LOCC using a minimal-dimensional entangled resource state. Clearly, here the entangled resource state provides an advantage irrespective of the dimension of the given set. Using this result, we also prove that any pure entangled state is useful as a resource to distinguish the states of any present set unambiguously with nonzero probability under LOCC. These sets exist in all two-qudit Hilbert spaces. Furthermore, it is possible to decrease the average entanglement content of such a set or to increase the cardinality of the set without changing certain properties of the same.


---


## 随机和量子动力学的几何基础

**Original Title:** Geometric Foundations of Stochastic and Quantum Dynamics

**Authors:** David V. Svintradze

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28292v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.28292v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-30


### 摘要

我们开发了随机动力学的几何公式，其中噪音、扩散、路径概率、波动定理和熵产生源于不断发展的多边形的内在几何，而不是源于外部强加的随机性。在移动动量理论中，我们建立了一种弯曲与噪音的对应关系：波动由逆弯曲张量决定，而熵产生由弯曲变形控制。移动超表面上的不变连续定律产生了几何福克-普朗克方程，而弯曲-速度耦合产生了确定路径权重的二次Onsager-Machlup函数。由此产生的熵函满足弯曲驱动的单调性定律，提供了第二定律的几何推导。在二维中，弯曲不变量简化为高斯弯曲并编码布局，因此布局转变会产生离散的熵跳变。当环境空间带有Minkowski特征时，产生消散热重的相同弯曲动力学二次型会产生振荡相重，并且控制信息演化的拉普拉斯-贝尔特拉米（Laplace-Beltrami）操作者获得薛定格型结构。这为经典随机行为和量子动力学之间的明显区别提供了几何分辨率。这些结果表明，随机行为、热力学不可逆性和量子转变幅度在移动的多边形框架内是统一的。几何不仅仅适应随机性;随机行为是确定性几何进化的结果。该理论预测了受弯曲控制的各向异性扩散、地形变化事件时的熵跳跃，以及几何热量子交叉，其中经典的随机权重和量子幅度是由相同的弯曲动力学作用产生的。


### Abstract

We develop a geometric formulation of stochastic dynamics in which noise, diffusion, path probabilities, fluctuation theorems, and entropy production arise from the intrinsic geometry of an evolving manifold rather than from externally imposed randomness. Within the theory of moving manifolds, we establish a curvature-noise correspondence: fluctuations are governed by the inverse curvature tensor, while entropy production is controlled by curvature deformation. The invariant continuity law on a moving hypersurface yields a geometric Fokker-Planck equation, and curvature-velocity coupling generates a quadratic Onsager-Machlup functional determining path weights. The resulting entropy functional satisfies a curvature-driven monotonicity law, providing a geometric derivation of the Second Law. In two dimensions, the curvature invariant reduces to Gaussian curvature and encodes topology, so topological transitions produce discrete entropy jumps. When the ambient space carries a Minkowskian signature, the same curvature-kinetic quadratic form that generates dissipative thermal weights produces oscillatory phase weights, and the Laplace-Beltrami operator governing entropy evolution acquires a Schrödinger-type structure. This provides a geometric resolution of the apparent distinction between classical stochastic behaviour and quantum dynamics. These results show that stochastic behaviour, thermodynamic irreversibility, and quantum transition amplitudes are unified within the moving manifold framework. Geometry does not merely accommodate stochasticity; stochastic behaviour arises as a consequence of deterministic geometric evolution. The theory predicts curvature-controlled anisotropic diffusion, entropy jumps at topology-changing events, and a geometric thermal-quantum crossover in which classical stochastic weights and quantum amplitudes are generated by the same curvature-kinetic action.


---


## 通过具有经典阴影的无监督域自适应从不完美量子数据中学习

**Original Title:** Learning from imperfect quantum data via unsupervised domain adaptation with classical shadows

**Authors:** Kosuke Ito, Akira Tanji, Hiroshi Yano, Yudai Suzuki, Naoki Yamamoto

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28294v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.28294v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-30


### 摘要

使用经典机器学习模型从量子数据中学习已成为实现量子优势的一个有希望的范式。尽管对其性能进行了广泛的分析，但在实际场景中，来自目标域的干净且完全标记的量子数据通常无法获得，这迫使模型根据在与部署时遇到的条件不同的条件下收集的数据进行训练。这种不匹配凸显了在先前工作的常见假设之外需要新方法。在这项工作中，我们通过采用无监督域适应框架从不完美量子数据中学习来解决这个问题。具体来说，通过利用通过经典阴影获得的量子状态的经典表示，一旦对量子状态执行测量，我们就完全在经典计算管道内执行无监督域自适应。我们在现实领域转移下对物质量子相和纠缠分类任务的框架进行了数值评估。在这两项任务中，我们的方法优于纯源非自适应基线和纯目标无监督学习方法，证明了领域适应对现实量子数据学习的实际适用性。


### Abstract

Learning from quantum data using classical machine learning models has emerged as a promising paradigm toward realizing quantum advantages. Despite extensive analyses on their performance, clean and fully labeled quantum data from the target domain are often unavailable in practical scenarios, forcing models to be trained on data collected under conditions that differ from those encountered at deployment. This mismatch highlights the need for new approaches beyond the common assumptions of prior work. In this work, we address this issue by employing an unsupervised domain adaptation framework for learning from imperfect quantum data. Specifically, by leveraging classical representations of quantum states obtained via classical shadows, we perform unsupervised domain adaptation entirely within a classical computational pipeline once measurements on the quantum states are executed. We numerically evaluate the framework on quantum phases of matter and entanglement classification tasks under realistic domain shifts. Across both tasks, our method outperforms source-only non-adaptive baselines and target-only unsupervised learning approaches, demonstrating the practical applicability of domain adaptation to realistic quantum data learning.


---


## 俘获离子计算机上的局部鲁棒阴影--案例研究

**Original Title:** Local robust shadows on a trapped ion computer -- a case study

**Authors:** Jadwiga Wilkens, Milena Guevara-Bertsch, Marwa Marso, Mederika Zangerl, Albert Frisch, Florian Girtler, Juris Ulmanis, Ingo Roth, Richard Kueng

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28307v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.28307v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-30


### 摘要

我们通过实验证明了捕获离子设备上的局部鲁棒阴影，这是一种为抵消测量误差而开发的协议。我们在校准阶段和阴影估计阶段之间交替，并在两个阶段的测量之前引入Pauli-X-旋转以对称错误率。然后，我们在被困离子量子计算机上演示了该协议，并人工缩短了测量脉冲持续时间。这会产生更快的实验，但代价是错误率增加，随后通过稳健的影子协议来缓解错误率。我们在三个示例性量子状态上对这种方法进行基准测试：局部哈尔随机状态，以及标准和保利相关编码的QAOA状态。在所有三种情况下，本地稳健影子协议都成功地减轻了由于测量脉冲持续时间较短而增加的错误率。


### Abstract

We experimentally demonstrate local robust shadows on a trapped-ion device, a protocol developed to counteract measurement errors. We alternate between a calibration stage and the shadow estimation stage and also introduce Pauli-X-twirling before measurements in both stages to symmetrize error rates. We then demonstrate the protocol on a trapped-ion quantum computer with artificially shortened measurement pulse duration. This yields faster experiments at the cost of increased error rates which are subsequently mitigated by the robust shadow protocol. We benchmark this approach on three exemplary quantum states: a local Haar random state, as well as standard and Pauli-correlation encoded QAOA states. In all three cases, the local robust shadow protocol succeeds at mitigating the increased error rates hailing from shorter measurement pulse durations.

## 采用单片集成硅光收发器的紧凑型连续可变量子密钥分发系统

**Original Title:** Compact Continuous-Variable Quantum Key Distribution System Employing Monolithically Integrated Silicon Photonic Transceiver

**Authors:** Denis Fatkhiev, João dos Reis Frazão, Alireza H. Derkani, Kadir Gümüş, Menno van den Hout, Aaron Albores-Mejia, Chigo Okonkwo

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28310v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.28310v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-30


### 摘要

我们展示了第一个CV-QKD系统，该系统具有定制设计的单片硅光双极化收发器。利用PS-64-QM，我们在25公里的标准单色光纤上实现了1.9 Mbit/s的密钥速率，凸显了电子-光集成在实际QKD中的潜力。


### Abstract

We demonstrate the first CV-QKD system featuring a custom-designed monolithic silicon photonic dual-polarisation transceiver. Leveraging PS-64-QAM, we achieved 1.9 Mbit/s secret key rate across 25 km of standard single-mode fibre, highlighting the potential of electronic-photonic integration for practical QKD.

## 用于鲁棒训练的高效量子算法

**Original Title:** Efficient Quantum Algorithm for Robust Training

**Authors:** Yue Wang, Guangyi He, Liepeng Zhang, Lukas Gonon, Qi Zhao

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28332v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.28332v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-30


### 摘要

对抗训练是安全关键机器学习系统中针对恶意输入扰动的标准防御。其主要负担是结构性的：在每次参数更新之前，必须首先攻击当前的模型以找到新的对抗性扰动，这使得训练变得越来越昂贵且难以在大模型规模上维持。在这里，我们给出了在局部稳定性和稀疏性假设下进行投影梯度鲁棒训练的端到端量子过程。关键步骤是将耦合攻击者-学习者动力学重新定义为一个多维稀疏线性系统，其终端块产生最终的网络参数状态。在此公式中，主要查询成本随着训练时间步线性扩展，最高可达对数因子，并随着模型大小呈多元关系，而完整门复杂性记录了单独的输入准备和稀疏访问管理费用。这将人工智能安全的核心计算任务置于具体的量子基础上，并确定了一种可以减少鲁棒训练费用的制度。


### Abstract

Adversarial training is a standard defense against malicious input perturbations in security-critical machine-learning systems. Its main burden is structural: before every parameter update, the current model must first be attacked to find a new adversarial perturbation, making training increasingly expensive and hard to sustain at large-model scale. Here we give an end-to-end quantum procedure for projected-gradient robust training under local stability and sparsity assumptions. The key step is to reformulate the coupled attacker--learner dynamics as a high-dimensional sparse linear system whose terminal block yields the final network-parameter state. In this formulation, the dominant query cost scales linearly with training time steps, up to logarithmic factors, and polylogarithmically with model size, while the full gate complexity records separate input-preparation and sparse-access overheads. This places core computational tasks for AI security on a concrete quantum footing and identifies a regime in which robust-training overhead can be reduced.


---


## 使用经典和量子方法分析甲醛

**Original Title:** Towards Analyzing Formic Acid Using Classical and Quantum Methods

**Authors:** Omer Gurevich, Tal Mor, Ido Ram

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28343v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.28343v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-30


### 摘要

催化碳固定到蚁酸对于研究减少碳足迹和生命的出现非常重要。离散量子详尽搜索与其他方法相结合能否帮助减少碳足迹？我们建议合并量子、量子启发和经典工具，以更好地模拟各种相关过程。量子工具经常用于分析分子的电子结构，有时是因为这个问题在经典计算机上不可扩展（轨道数量），而在（未来的）量子计算机上它可能大致可扩展。它甚至有可能在不久的将来使用变分量子本征解器（VQE）来解决，但此类分析的一个主要障碍是描述该问题的希尔伯特空间中出现贫瘠的高原。   在这里，我们利用基本（标准）工具，同时还包括一种新颖的工具--离散量子详尽搜索，它依赖于相互无偏的基础，用于分析涉及二氧化碳、氢和蚁酸的最简单的非催化过程。


### Abstract

Catalytic carbon fixation to formic acid is important for studying the reduction of carbon footprint and the emergence of life. Can discrete quantum exhaustive search merged with other methods help reduce the carbon footprint? We suggest merging quantum, quantum inspired, and classical tools for a better simulation of various relevant processes. Quantum tools are often used for analyzing the electronic structure of molecules, sometimes because this problem is not scalable (in the number of orbitals) on classical computers while it is potentially approximately scalable on (future) quantum computers. It is potentially even solvable in the near future using variational quantum eigensolvers (VQE) yet a major obstacle to such analysis is the appearance of barren plateaus in the Hilbert space describing the problem.
  Here we make use of the basic (standard) tools while also including a novel one -- the discrete quantum exhaustive search, which relies on mutually unbiased bases, for analyzing the simplest non-catalytic process involving carbon dioxide, hydrogen and formic acid.

## 全局张量网络本征态的局部刻画

**Original Title:** The local characterization of global tensor network eigenstates

**Authors:** José Garre Rubio, András Molnár, Norbert Schuch, Frank Verstraete

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28349v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.28349v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-30


### 摘要

我们研究矩阵积状态（MPS）或矩阵积运算符是广义局部运算符（例如Hamilton）的精确本征载体的条件。通过适当地选择局部操作符，这涵盖了广泛的设置：汉密尔顿的精确本征状态，包括疤痕状态、驱动量子系统的精确MPS轨迹、局部Lindbladians的稳态、汉密尔顿或密度矩阵的广义对称性等等。我们的关键结果是，一个局部的固定大小方程--即运算符中的单个项如何作用于一组张量--为精确解提供了充分的必要条件。这使得可以描述所有上述问题的全部解决方案，并通过分析和数字方式识别它们。我们详细介绍了这种特征化在所有上述设置中的具体应用，特别是通过使用它来恢复XXZ模型的量子群对称性来验证我们的局部特征化的力量。我们还讨论了MPS在数值算法中的应用以及我们的结果到2D的推广，即投射纠缠对状态（PEPS）。


### Abstract

We study the conditions under which Matrix Product States (MPS) or Matrix Product Operators are exact eigenvectors of an extensive local operator, such as a Hamiltonian. By suitably choosing the local operator, this covers a wide range of settings: Exact eigenstates of Hamiltonians, including scar states, exact MPS trajectories for driven quantum systems, steady states of local Lindbladians, generalized symmetries of either Hamiltonians or density matrices, and many more. Our key result is that that a local, fixed-size equation -- namely, how a single term in the operator acts on a block of tensors -- provides a necessary and sufficient condition for exact solutions. This allows to characterize the full space of solutions in all of the aforementioned problems, and to identify them both analytically and numerically. We elaborate on the concrete application of this characterization to all of the aforementioned settings, and in particular exemplify the power of our local characterization by using it to recover the quantum group symmetries of the XXZ model. We also discuss applications to numerical algorithms with MPS and the generalization of our results to 2D, i.e., projected entangled pair states (PEPS).


---


## 费米黄金法则的透视及其在化学物理学中的推广

**Original Title:** Perspective of Fermi's golden rule and its generalizations in chemical physics

**Authors:** Seogjoo J. Jang, Goun Kim, Young Min Rhee

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28373v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.28373v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-30


### 摘要

这个角度提供了费米黄金法则（FGR）的简洁历史，概述了其推导、假设和代表形式。回顾了FGR的主要应用，主要在化学物理领域。这些说明了FGR的广泛适用性和成功。澄清了FGR实际应用中遇到的模糊性和悬而未决的问题。讨论了FGR推广和实际应用计算方法的最新进展。


### Abstract

This perspective provides a succinct history of Fermi's golden rule (FGR), overview of its derivation, assumptions, and representative forms. Major applications of FGR, mostly in the field of chemical physics, are reviewed. These illustrate the broad applicability and success of FGR. Ambiguities and open issues encountered in practical applications of FGR are clarified. Recent advances in generalizations of FGR and computational methods for practical applications are addressed.

## 真空涨落引起的核子之间的吸引力

**Original Title:** The force of attraction between nucleons due to vacuum fluctuation

**Authors:** Anupam Ghosh

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28379v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.28379v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-30


### 摘要

在这封信中，我们推导出了两个平行金属板之间的相互作用能和力，它们是由当它们彼此非常接近时的量子真空涨落产生的。我们认为真空由一个强子场组成。在量子强子动力学中，强子是核力的载体。


### Abstract

In this letter, we derive the interaction energy and the force between two parallel metal plates, arising from quantum vacuum fluctuations when they are very close to each other. We consider the vacuum to be composed of a meson field. In Quantum Hadrodynamics, mesons are the carriers of the nuclear force.

## 基于Bayesian优化和最大概率评估的资源高效量子逼近优化算法

**Original Title:** Resource-efficient quantum approximate optimization algorithm via Bayesian optimization and maximum-probability evaluation

**Authors:** Siran Zhang, Shuming Cheng

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28413v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.28413v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-30


### 摘要

量子逼近优化算法（QAOA）是组合优化的领先变分方法，但其实际性能很大程度上取决于目标设计、参数搜索和镜头分配。我们提出了一个资源高效的QAOA框架，该框架使用最可能测量位串的切割值作为优化目标，将其与Bayesian优化相结合，并根据模式置信度和标准化切割值方差使用双重标准自适应地分配镜头。对3-常规MaxCut的数值实验表明，对于未加权和加权实例，所提出的方案都实现了与传统基于期望的目标相当的离散解质量，同时通常需要更少的总射击才能达到相同的最终模式准确性。这些结果表明，围绕最大概率位串重新组织QAOA为在有限的测量预算下提高实际性能提供了有效途径。


### Abstract

The quantum approximate optimization algorithm (QAOA) is a leading variational approach to combinatorial optimization, but its practical performance depends strongly on objective design, parameter search, and shot allocation. We present a resource-efficient QAOA framework that uses the cut value of the most probable measured bitstring as the optimization objective, combines it with Bayesian optimization, and adaptively allocates shots using dual criteria based on mode confidence and normalized cut-value variance. Numerical experiments on 3-regular MaxCut show that, for both unweighted and weighted instances, the proposed scheme achieves discrete-solution quality comparable to that of the conventional expectation-based objective while typically requiring fewer total shots to reach the same final mode accuracy. These results indicate that reorganizing QAOA around the maximum-probability bitstring provides an effective route to improving practical performance under limited measurement budgets.

## 学习磁力测量原子量子中内部旋转压缩的统一控制

**Original Title:** Learning unified control of internal spin squeezing in atomic qudits for magnetometry

**Authors:** C. Z. Cao, J. Z. Han, M. Xiong, M. Deng, L. Wang, X. Lv, M. Xue

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2603.28421v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2603.28421v1

**Submitted:** 2026-03-30


### 摘要

产生和保留计量有用的量子状态是量子增强原子磁力测量的核心挑战。在低场区域运行的多层原子中，非线性塞曼（NLZ）效应既是一种资源，也是一种限制。它非线性地重新分配内部旋转涨落，以在单个原子量子密度内产生旋转压缩状态，但在固定读出下，它会扭曲与测量相关的积分并限制可访问的拉曼放大。挤压轴和有效非线性作用的时间依赖性加剧了这一挑战。在这里，我们表明，基于物理信息的强化学习可以将NLZ动态从读出退化的来源转化为持续的可重写资源。仅使用实验上可访问的低级旋转矩，训练有素的代理在$^{161}\mathrm{DY}$的$f=21/2$中识别出一种统一的控制策略，该策略可以快速准备强压缩的内部状态并在始终在线的NLZ进化下稳定超过$4，mathrm {DB}$的固定轴旋转压缩。包括状态准备费用在内，学习到的协议产生的单原子磁灵敏度为$13.9\，\mathrm {pT}/\SQRT{\mathrm{Hz}}$，对应于超过标准量子限制约$3\，\mathrm {DB}$的优势。我们的结果确立了基于学习的控制作为将多层量子传感器中不可避免的固有非线性动力学转化为操作可扩展优势的实用途径。


### Abstract

Generating and preserving metrologically useful quantum states is a central challenge in quantum-enhanced atomic magnetometry. In multilevel atoms operated in the low-field regime, the nonlinear Zeeman (NLZ) effect is both a resource and a limitation. It nonlinearly redistributes internal spin fluctuations to generate spin-squeezed states within a single atomic qudit, yet under fixed readout it distorts the measurement-relevant quadrature and limits the accessible metrological gain. This challenge is compounded by the time dependence of both the squeezing axis and the effective nonlinear action. Here we show that physics-informed reinforcement learning can transform NLZ dynamics from a source of readout degradation into a sustained metrological resource. Using only experimentally accessible low-order spin moments, a trained agent identifies, in the $f=21/2$ manifold of $^{161}\mathrm{Dy}$, a unified control policy that rapidly prepares strongly squeezed internal states and stabilizes more than $4\,\mathrm{dB}$ of fixed-axis spin squeezing under always-on NLZ evolution. Including state-preparation overhead, the learned protocol yields a single-atom magnetic sensitivity of $13.9\,\mathrm{pT}/\sqrt{\mathrm{Hz}}$, corresponding to an advantage of approximately $3\,\mathrm{dB}$ beyond the standard quantum limit. Our results establish learning-based control as a practical route for converting unavoidable intrinsic nonlinear dynamics in multilevel quantum sensors into operational metrological advantage.
